321      
322    /**
323     * moving away from simple on/off flag as there could be multiple trades, i.e. more than one flavor of createTrade(),
324     * within the same lock/transaction because of multiple price-points, odd & mixed lot..etc scenarios.
325     * we need to track all the create operations within the lock/transaction in order to properly 
326     * synchronize the cancel publishing for cancel that takes place at the end of the lock/transaction 
327     * depending on the scenario or trade(s) outcome.
328     * The initial value 0 indicates NO asynchronous trade is pending. The value is incremented each time the 
329     * tradable is updated and decremented, when the explicit asynchronous cancel publish is called, 
330     * after the tradable's fill generation and publishing.
331     */
332    //private transient volatile boolean asyncCreateTradePending = false;
333    private transient volatile int asyncCreateTradePending = 0;
334    
335    // cancel reports pending because of ongoing asynchronous create trade

337    //private transient ArrayList<CancelReturnContext> pendingCxReturns = new ArrayList<CancelReturnContext>();

353        }
354    }

403    /**
404     * New constructor added for handling Light orders. 
405     * @author josephg
406     */
407        public OrderImpl (LightOrderEntry newOrder, SessionProfileUserStruct userStruct, TradingProduct product, String correspondent) throws DataValidationException,SystemException
408        {
409                 
410                if (correspondent == null)
411                {
412                        throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Correspondent could not be found/generated for user: " + userStruct.userId, 0);
413                }
414//                 initFromRequest(newOrder);
415                originalQuantity = newOrder.getQuantity();
416                userAssignedId = newOrder.getUserAssignedId();
417                cmtaExchange = newOrder.getCmtaExchange();
418        cmtaFirm = newOrder.getCmtaFirmNumber();
419        side = newOrder.getSide();
420        orderOriginType = (char) newOrder.getOriginCode();
421        userId = newOrder.getUserId();
422        userKey = findUserKey(newOrder.getUserId());
423        positionEffect = newOrder.getPositionEffect();
424        coverage = newOrder.getCoverage();
425        if (newOrder.isImmediateOrCancel())
426        {
427                contingency = ioc_contingency;
428        }
429        else
430        {
431                contingency = no_contingency;
432        }
433        price = newOrder.getPrice();
434        contingencyPrice = PriceFactory.create(PriceTypes.NO_PRICE, 0);        
435        boolean nbboProtected = newOrder.nbboProtectionOn();
436        if (nbboProtected)
437        {
438                orderNBBOProtectionType = OrderNBBOProtectionTypes.FULL;
439        }
440        else
441        {
442                orderNBBOProtectionType = OrderNBBOProtectionTypes.NONE;
443        }                
444        setHadNBBOProtection(nbboProtected); //TODO ???
445        setTransactionSequenceNumber(0);
446        String pdpm = newOrder.getPdpm();
447        if (pdpm != null && pdpm.length() > 0)
448        {
449                setExtensions(PDPMExtensionsCompatibleHelper.TIERED_PDPM_KEY + pdpm);
450        }
451        else
452        {
453                setExtensions("");
454        }
455        setLastBookedPrice(price);
456 
457        
458//                 initFromProfile (userStruct);
459                SessionProfileStruct lightOrderProfile = 
460                        UserProfileHelper.getUserProfileForClass(userStruct, product.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey(), product.getTradingClass().getSessionName());
461                
462        optionalData = "";
463        account = lightOrderProfile.account;
464        subaccount = lightOrderProfile.subAccount;
465        userAcronym = userStruct.userAcronym;
466        originator = userStruct.userAcronym;
467 
468                
469//                 initFromProduct (product);
470        activeSession = product.getTradingClass().getSessionName();
471                // create orderId by contacting ID service
472                orderKey = LightOrderUtils.generateOrderId();
473        UuidHolder uuid = new UuidHolder(orderKey);
474        sourceReceivedTime = System.currentTimeMillis(); //TODO or nano? also do we need this set?
475        
476        
477                orderId = new OrderIdStruct(lightOrderProfile.executingGiveupFirm, newOrder.getBranch(), 
478                                        newOrder.getBranchSequence(), correspondent, LightOrderUtils.getDate(sourceReceivedTime), uuid.getPrimaryBytes(),uuid.getSecondaryBytes());
479                classKey = product.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey();
480        productKey = product.getProductKey();
481 
482        productType = product.getTradingClass().getProductType();
483        sessionNames = new String[1];
484        sessionNames[0] = activeSession;
485                 
486//                 initCommonFields();
487                timeInForce = TimesInForce.DAY;
488                bookedQuantity = 0;
489        cancelledQuantity = 0;
490        tradedQuantity = 0;
491        bustedQuantity = 0;
492        source = Sources.LIGHT; 
493                
494        ohsReceivedTime = 0;
495        addedQuantity = 0;
496        orsId = "";
497        setBookedTime(0L);
498        setBookedStatus(0);
499        setWidenPrice(null); // this is initialized in OrderHomeImpl.setTransientValues to noPrice first
500        setShipQuantityWithoutPublishing(0);
501        setMarketAlertPublished(false);
502        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
503        setPendingTradePrice(null);
504        setPendingTradeId(0);
505        setInvolvedInQuoteTrigger(false);
506        setCancelRequestPending(false);
507        setPendingCancelRequestUserAssignedId(null);
508        setPendingCancelQuantity(0);
509        setCancelReplaceNewOrder(null);
510        markForDropCopy(false);
511        setBookedByAuction(false);
512        setInitialTradePrice(null);
513        setOddLotFlashedQuantity(0);
514 
515        setFillType(SubActivityType.DEFAULT);
516        markAuctionStarted(false);
517        setMarkedCancelReason((short)0);
518        setState(OrderStates.ACTIVE); //TODO what state to start with?
519        legOrderDetails = emptyLegDetails;
520        
521        }
522    
523    /**
524     * This method populates the Order attributes that make an Order unique. Attributes that are part of the Order ID
525     * author Silvia Torres
526     */
527    private void setNonUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)
528            throws DataValidationException,SystemException
529    {
530        activeSession = newValues.activeSession;
531        timeInForce = newValues.timeInForce;
532        orderId = newValues.orderId;
533        classKey = newValues.classKey;
534        originalQuantity = newValues.originalQuantity;
535        userAssignedId = newValues.userAssignedId;
536        ohsReceivedTime = newValues.ohsReceivedTime;
537        sourceReceivedTime = newValues.sourceReceivedTime;
538        side = newValues.side;
539        setOrderSide(newValues.side);
540        source = newValues.source;
541        orderOriginType = newValues.orderOriginType;
542        addedQuantity = newValues.addedQuantity;
543        coverage = newValues.coverage;
544        originator = newValues.originator;
545        orsId = newValues.orsId;
546        positionEffect = newValues.positionEffect;
547        productKey = newValues.productKey;
548        productType = newValues.productType;
549        subaccount = newValues.subaccount;
550        userId = newValues.userId;
551        sessionNames = newValues.sessionNames;
552        contingency = newValues.contingency;
553        orderNBBOProtectionType = newValues.orderNBBOProtectionType;
554        userKey = findUserKey(newValues.userId);
555        contingencyPrice = PriceFactory.create(newValues.contingency.price);
556        orderKey = CboeId.longValue(new CboeIdStruct(newValues.orderId.highCboeId, newValues.orderId.lowCboeId));
557        userAcronym = findUser(newValues.userId).userAcronym;
558    }
559 
560   protected SessionProfileUserStruct findUser(String userId) throws SystemException, DataValidationException
561    {
562        try
563        {
564            return BusinessServicesHelper.getUserService().getSessionProfileUserInformation(userId);
565        }
566        catch (AuthorizationException ex)
567        {
568            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Authorization exception finding user by id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
569        }
570        catch (NotFoundException ex)
571        {
572            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid user id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
573        }
574        catch (CommunicationException ex)
575        {
576            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Communication exception finding user by id " + userId + ": " + ex + ": " + ex.details.message, 0);
577        }
578    }
579 
580    /**
581     * The update Order process must be consistent with TPF. So, the only fields that need
582     * to be updated and checked are Optional data, Account and cmta.
583     * author Silvia Torres
584     */
585    private void setUserUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)
586    {
587        setOptionalData( newValues.optionalData );
588        setAccount( newValues.account );
589        setSubAccount(newValues.subaccount);
590        setCmtaExchange( newValues.cmta.exchange );
591        setCmta( newValues.cmta.firmNumber );
592    }
593 
594    private void setSystemUpdateableValues(OrderHandlingStruct order)
595    {
596        // persisted field
597        setCancelledQuantity(order.cancelledQuantity);
598        setTradedQuantity(order.tradedQuantity);
599        setHadNBBOProtection(order.hadNBBOProtection);
600        setState(order.state);
601        setPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.price));
602        setLastBookedPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.effectivePrice));
603        setTransactionSequenceNumber(order.transactionSequenceNumber);
604        setExtensions(order.extensions);
605        setBustedQuantity(order.bustedQuantity);
606 
607        setBookedTime(0L);
608        setBookedStatus(0);
609        setWidenPrice(null); // this is initialized in OrderHomeImpl.setTransientValues to noPrice first
610        setShipQuantityWithoutPublishing(0);
611        setMarketAlertPublished(false);
612        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
613        setPendingTradePrice(null);
614        setPendingTradeId(0);
615        setInvolvedInQuoteTrigger(false);
616        setCancelRequestPending(false);
617        setPendingCancelRequestUserAssignedId(null);
618        setPendingCancelQuantity(0);
619        setCancelReplaceNewOrder(null);
620        markForDropCopy(false);
621        setBookedByAuction(false);
622        setInitialTradePrice(null);
623        setBookedQuantity(0);
624        setOddLotFlashedQuantity(0);
625 
626        setFillType(SubActivityType.DEFAULT);
627        markAuctionStarted(false);
628        setMarkedCancelReason((short)0);
629 
630        if(!order.handlingInstruction.equals(""))
631        {
632            HandlingInstruction handlingInstructionImpl = new OrderHandlingInstructionNoReflectionImpl();
633            handlingInstructionImpl.updateFrom(order.handlingInstruction, getQuantity());
634            setHandlingInstruction(handlingInstructionImpl);
635            expressOrder = handlingInstructionImpl.isExpressOrder();
636            this.inboundISOEnabled = handlingInstructionImpl.isInboundISOEnabled();
637            setBookableOrderMarketLimit(handlingInstructionImpl.getBookableOrderMarketLimit());
638        }
639    }
640 
641    public void acceptOrderUpdateFromSync(OrderHandlingStruct order) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
642    {
643        // persisted field
644        setCancelledQuantity(order.cancelledQuantity);
645        setTradedQuantity(order.tradedQuantity);
646        setHadNBBOProtection(order.hadNBBOProtection);
647        setState(order.state);
648        setPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.price));
649        //setLastBookedPrice(PriceFactory.create(order.effectivePrice));
650        setTransactionSequenceNumber(order.transactionSequenceNumber);
651        setExtensions(order.extensions);
652        setBustedQuantity(order.bustedQuantity);
653 
654        if(!order.handlingInstruction.equals(""))
655        {
656            HandlingInstruction handlingInstructionImpl = new OrderHandlingInstructionNoReflectionImpl();
657            handlingInstructionImpl.updateFrom(order.handlingInstruction, getQuantity());
658            setHandlingInstruction(handlingInstructionImpl);
659            expressOrder = handlingInstructionImpl.isExpressOrder();
660            this.inboundISOEnabled = handlingInstructionImpl.isInboundISOEnabled();
661            setBookableOrderMarketLimit(handlingInstructionImpl.getBookableOrderMarketLimit());
662        }     
663        setOptionalData( order.optionalData );
664        setAccount( order.account );
665        setSubAccount(order.subaccount);
666        setCmtaExchange( order.cmta.exchange );
667        setCmta( order.cmta.firmNumber );
668    }

670    /**
671     * Set all fields of the persistent OrderImpl from a given OrderStruct.
672     * <p/>
673     * author Steven Sinclair
674     *
675     * @param order com.cboe.businessServices.interfaces.orderHandlingService.OrderStruct
676     */
677    public void setOrder(OrderHandlingStruct order) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
678    {
679        setNonUpdateableValues(order);
680        setSystemUpdateableValues(order);
681        setUserUpdateableValues(order);
682    }

721    public String getExecutingBroker()
722    {
723        // if clears like quote use originator's setup (new requirement for I-order 2-25-04), otherwise use default setup
724        if (clearsLikeQuote())
725        {
726            if (Log.isDebugOn())
727            {
728                Log.debug(this, "getExecutingBroker for I-Order: " + toString() + " use originator: " + getOriginatorAcronym().acronym);
729            }
730            return getOriginatorAcronym().acronym; // this could be the use or the originator is has one
731        }
732        else
733        {
734            return getMyHome().getExecutingBroker();
735        }

738    private int getOriginalQuantity(boolean noCalculation)
739    {
740        if(noCalculation) return originalQuantity;
741        
742        if(isCrossProductLegOrder())
743        {
744            return getCrossProductLegOrderQuantity();
745        }
746        return originalQuantity;
747    }

753 
754    /**
755     * if the quanity is defined in the extensions field use it.
756     * @return
757     */
758    private int getCrossProductLegOrderQuantity()
759    {
760        try
761        {
762            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(getExtensions());
763            String strQuantityToTrade = extensionsHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_QUANTITY);
764            if(strQuantityToTrade != null)
765            {    
766                return Integer.parseInt(extensionsHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_QUANTITY));
767            }
768        }
769        catch(Exception e)
770        {
771            // no need to worry about this since it might not be set.
772        }
773        return originalQuantity;
774    }
775    
776    public int getCrossProductRatioQuantity()
777    {
778        if (crossProductRatioQuantity != 0)
779        {
780            return crossProductRatioQuantity;
781        }
782        
783        if(isCrossProductLegOrder())
784        {
785            try
786            {
787                ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(getExtensions());
788                String strQuantityToTrade = extensionsHelper.getValue(InternalExtensionFields.EQUITY_LEG_RATIO_QTY);
789                if(strQuantityToTrade != null)
790                {    
791                    crossProductRatioQuantity = Integer.parseInt(extensionsHelper.getValue(InternalExtensionFields.EQUITY_LEG_RATIO_QTY));
792                    return crossProductRatioQuantity;
793                }
794            }
795            catch(Exception e)
796            {   
797                //no need to worry about this since it might not be set.
798                if(Log.isDebugOn())
799                {
800                    Log.debug("OrderImpl.getCrossProductRatioQuantity> Ratio not already set.");
801                }
802            }
803        }
804        return 0;  
805    }

944    public void setState(short aValue) 
945    {
946        short oldState = getState();
947        if (isBypassReflection())
948        {
949            state = aValue;
950        }
951        else
952        {
953            getCurrentTXLog().setState(this.state);
954            state = aValue;
955        }
956 
957        if (oldState != 0) // Since if it setting the state at creation of OrderImpl object we do
958            // not
959            // want to call this mthod.
960            publishInternalStateChange(oldState, aValue);
961        //If the remaining quantity is less than or equal to zero add it to a list to be removed later
962        //this will take care of deleting ONLY cancelled orders
963        if (getRemainingQuantity() <= 0 && getTradedQuantity() <=0) {
964                        try {
965                                getTradingClass(getClassKey()).addToToBeRemovedOrders(this);
966                        } catch (DataValidationException e) {
967                                Log.alarm("Unable to get TradingClass" + e);
968                        }
969        }
970    }

975    }

1559/**
1560 * Gets time contingency status.  Only currently supported time continengencies
1561 * (for orders traded in SBT) are IOC, FOK.  If boolean to ignore handling instruction, the
1562 * real contingency type will be returned, otherwise will return it based on the handing instruction.
1563 * 
1564 */
1565public boolean hasTimeContingency(boolean ifConsiderHandlingInstruction) {
1566    if (ifConsiderHandlingInstruction && getHandlingInstruction() != null && getHandlingInstruction().ignoreContingency()) {
1567        return false;
1568    }
1569    return getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.IOC || getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.FOK;
1570}
1571/**
1572 * Gets volume contingency status.  Only currently supported volume continengencies
1573 * (for orders traded in SBT) are AON and FOK.  If boolean to ignore handling instruction, the
1574 * real contingency type will be returned, otherwise will return it based on the handing instruction.
1575 * 
1576 */
1577public boolean hasVolumeContingency(boolean ifConsiderHandlingInstruction) {
1578    if (ifConsiderHandlingInstruction && getHandlingInstruction() != null && getHandlingInstruction().ignoreContingency()) {
1579        return false;
1580    }
1581    return getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.AON || getRealContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.FOK;
1582}

1617/**
1618 * External source has booked the order.  No need to change the state, just log the history
1619 */
1620public void acceptedByBookExternal()
1621{
1622    // probably called by an external book... just use current time as booked time
1623    acceptedByBook( TimeServiceWrapper.getCurrentDateTimeInMillis(), getPrice(), true, false);
1624}
1625 
1626public void acceptedByBook(long aBookedTime, Price bookedPrice, boolean silent)
1627{
1628    acceptedByBook(aBookedTime, bookedPrice, false, silent);
1629}
1630 
1631public void acceptedByBook(long aBookedTime, Price bookedPrice, boolean isExternalUpdate, boolean silent)
1632{
1633        Price initialValue = getLastBookedPrice();
1634        Price finalValue = bookedPrice;
1635        setLastBookedPrice(bookedPrice);
1636     
1637        if(!silent)
1638        {
1639            setHandlingInstruction(null); //after booked, original handling instruction should not used
1640        }
1641        
1642    // will be accepted by book each time recovery is done, only need to
1643    // create booked history and publish if quantity is changing
1644 
1645        // only update the state if is booked at CBOEDirect.  Do not update state for external book since we did not book it here
1646            if (!isExternalUpdate)
1647        {
1648            setState(OrderStates.BOOKED);
1649        }
1650 
1651        if (isLightOrder())
1652        {
1653                    LightOrderBookedEventCodec bookedEventCodec = LightOrderBookedEventCodec.getInstance();
1654                    bookedEventCodec.reset();
1655                    bookedEventCodec.setBookedQuantity(bookedQuantity);
1656                    bookedEventCodec.setBookedTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
1657 
1658                byte[] bookedEvent = LightOrderBuffer.getThreadLocalInstance().encode(bookedEventCodec);
1659                // publish a booked event for light order and return
1660                getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, 
1661                                InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptLightOrderEvent.getEventType()).acceptLightOrderEvent(
1662                                                        getRoutingStruct().groups[0], orderKey, bookedEvent);
1663                
1664                return;
1665        }
1666        
1667        // Check the flag to see if order needs to publish book event and store history
1668                      
1669        boolean isStopOrder = getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP
1670            || getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP_LIMIT
1671        || getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.STP_LOSS;
1672        
1673        boolean isToPublishToExternal = (!silent) && (needPublishBookedEvent() || isStopOrder || (!finalValue.equals(initialValue)));
1674           
1675        if ( isToPublishToExternal) 
1676        {
1677                incrementSequenceNumber();
1678                MarketDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs = buildMarketDetailStructs();
1679                getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptedByOrderBook.getEventType()).acceptedByOrderBook(
1680                                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1681                                getOrderId(), OrderStates.BOOKED,
1682                                getOrderBookUpdateStruct(), 
1683                                isToPublishToExternal, getPrimitiveProductKey(), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1684                                ordHistoryStructs);
1685                setNeedPublishBookedEvent(false);
1686        }
1687 
1688        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1689        {
1690            Log.debug(this, "OrderAcceptedByBook, UserId: " + getUserId() + "  Order Id: " + orderIdToString(getOrderId()));
1691        }
1692        }
1693 
1694/**
1695     * This method publishes the intermediate Order states over the IOSC to OHS.
1696     * @param oldState
1697     * @param newState
1698     */
1699    private void publishInternalStateChange(short oldState, short newState)
1700    {
1701        /**
1702         * If the state is routed away then return
1703         */
1704        if(newState == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY) {
1705            return;
1706        }
1707        if( (oldState != newState) && (newState != OrderStates.BOOKED &&
1708                                       newState != OrderStates.ACTIVE &&
1709                                       newState != OrderStates.CANCEL &&
1710                                       newState != OrderStates.FILL))
1711        {
1712            com.cboe.idl.order.MarketDetailStruct[] ordDetails = buildMarketDetailStructs();
1713            getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptInternalStateUpdate.getEventType()).acceptInternalStateUpdate(
1714                    getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
1715                    getOrderId(), newState, getPrimitiveProductKey(), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
1716                    ordDetails);            
1717        }
1718    }
1719

1723    /**
1724     * author Steven Sinclair
1725     */
1726    public void activate()
1727    {

1729    }
1730 
1731    /**
1732     * parTradeMMSideBust will come from the BustReportManager. This will tell the order if the bust if coming
1733     * from a par trade and is the market maker executing the bust.  For these trade busts we do not want to publish
1734     * the bust report to the CMI user, however we want to publish the bust report to OHS so that a notification
1735     * can be sent to the OMT through the ReportWorkflow
1736     */
1737    public void bust(BustReportStruct bustInfo, TradeReport tradeReport, boolean parTradeMMSideBust) throws DataValidationException
1738    {
1739        // add this order to the cache so when it is reinstated, it will look at the same copy or the orderimpl
1740        // otherwise the reinstate will look at the database copy.
1741//        addOrderToCache();        
1742        if (bustInfo.productKey == getPrimitiveProductKey())
1743        {
1744                doOrderBust(bustInfo);
1745                bustInfo.bustReportType = getReportType();
1746        }
1747        else
1748        {
1749                doLegBust(bustInfo);
1750                bustInfo.bustReportType = ReportTypes.STRATEGY_LEG_REPORT;
1751        }
1752        bustInfo.transactionSequenceNumber = incrementSequenceNumber();
1753        publishBustReport(bustInfo, tradeReport, parTradeMMSideBust);
1754    }
1755 
1756    /**
1757     * This method will bust the specifed quantity.  This reduces traded quantity and increase busted quantity
1758     */
1759    public void bust(BustReportStruct bustInfo, TradeReport tradeReport) throws DataValidationException
1760    {
1761        bust(bustInfo, tradeReport, false); // false should always publish the bust report out from TE.
1762    }
1763 
1764    public void bust(BustReportStruct bustInfo) throws DataValidationException
1765    {
1766        bust(bustInfo, null);
1767    }
1768 
1769    /**
1770    * do order bust
1771    */
1772    private void doOrderBust(BustReportStruct bustInfo) throws DataValidationException
1773    {
1774                int quantity = bustInfo.bustedQuantity;
1775        if (quantity > getTradedQuantity())
1776        {
1777            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot bust more than the traded quantity",
1778                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
1779        }
1780        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1781        {
1782            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] Execute a bust on order for quantity " + quantity);
1783            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] traded/bust/cancelled is currently " + getTradedQuantity() + "/" + getBustedQuantity() + "/" + getCancelledQuantity());
1784        }
1785        setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() - quantity);
1786        setBustedQuantity(getBustedQuantity() + quantity);
1787        setCancelledQuantity(getCancelledQuantity() + quantity); //Since busted is no longer used in calculating remains, the cancelled quantity is incremented to account for the change.
1788        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1789        {
1790            Log.debug(this, "[orderId=" + getOrderId() + "] traded/bust/cancelled adjusted to " + getTradedQuantity() + "/" + getBustedQuantity() + "/" + getCancelledQuantity());
1791        }
1792        }
1793 
1794        /**
1795         * find the leg detail and ask it to finish the leg bust
1796         */
1797    private void doLegBust(BustReportStruct bustInfo) throws DataValidationException
1798    {
1799        try
1800        {
1801                        LegOrderDetailImpl legDetail = (LegOrderDetailImpl) findOrderDetailForLeg(bustInfo.productKey);
1802                        legDetail.bust(bustInfo);
1803                }
1804        catch (Exception e)
1805        {
1806            Log.exception("can not do leg bust (product key is " + bustInfo.productKey + ")", e);
1807                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Can not do leg bust for order " + getOrderIdString(), 0);
1808                }
1809        }
1810 
1811// CBOEdirect Stock System uses this to identify Order from ITS.
1812//10/21/02 Ravi Rade Added to check if order is a linkage order.
1813 
1814public boolean isLinkageOrder()
1815{
1816    boolean linkageOrder = false;
1817    final char originType = getOrderOriginType();
1818    final char theSource = getSource();    
1819    if (getActiveSession().equals(CBSX_SESSION))  {
1820        if ((getUserAssignedId() != null) &&
1821            getUserAssignedId().equals(Order.SYSTEM_LINK_ORDER_USER_ASSIGNED_ID))  {
1822            linkageOrder = true;
1823        }
1824        else if (((originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL) ||
1825                (originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT)) &&
1826                (theSource == Sources.ITS))  {
1827            linkageOrder = true;                   
1828        }
1829    }
1830    else {
1831        if (originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL ||
1832                originType == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT ||
1833                originType == OrderOrigins.SATISFACTION)  {
1834            linkageOrder = true;
1835        }
1836    }
1837    return linkageOrder;
1838}

1916     */
1917    private boolean propagateToOrderLegs()
1918    {

1921        {

1924        catch (NotFoundException e)

1931        /**
1932         * publish cancel reports
1933     * <p/>
1934         * Note: cancelRequestId is only used for order which had NBBO protection.
1935         *       for normal cancel, it should be set to 0
1936         */
1937    public synchronized void publishCancelReports(CancelReportStruct[] reports, short cancelReason, long cancelRequestId, boolean p_reportsUnconditionally)
1938    {
1939            if (Log.isDebugOn())
1940                {
1941                        Log.debug(this, "publishCancelReports - Order [orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + "]. Pending ASYNC_TRADE = "+asyncCreateTradePending);
1942                }
1943                
1944        if(asyncCreateTradePending > 0)
1945        {
1946                for(CancelReportStruct report : reports)
1947                {
1948                        adjustTotalSessionCancelledQuantity(report.cancelledQuantity);
1949                }
1950 
1951                OrderCancelCommand catCommand = OrderCancelCommand.getInstance();
1952                catCommand.setCancelContext(this, reports, cancelReason, cancelRequestId);
1953                catCommand.setOrderStruct(this.getOrderStruct());
1954 
1955                //CancelContext cxContext = new CancelContext(reports, cancelReason, cancelRequestId);  
1956                //pendingCxReports.add(cxContext);
1957        }
1958        else
1959        {        
1960                directPublishCancelReports(reports, cancelReason, cancelRequestId, false, null);
1961        }
1962    }
1963    
1964    public void directPublishCancelReports(CancelReportStruct[] reports, short cancelReason, long cancelRequestId, boolean updateTXNSqNumb, OrderStruct os)
1965    {
1966        long activityTime = System.currentTimeMillis(); 
1967                
1968        if(!updateTXNSqNumb) // only if synchronous 
1969        {
1970        for(CancelReportStruct report : reports)
1971        {
1972            adjustTotalSessionCancelledQuantity(report.cancelledQuantity);
1973        }
1974        }
1975            
1976            int txnSeqNumb = getTransactionSequenceNumber();
1977            
1978            CancelStruct[] cxStructs = null;
1979            if(updateTXNSqNumb)
1980            {
1981                    txnSeqNumb = incrementSequenceNumber();
1982                    
1983                    for(int i=0; i < reports.length; i++)
1984            {
1985                 reports[i].transactionSequenceNumber = txnSeqNumb;
1986            }
1987                    
1988                    os.transactionSequenceNumber = txnSeqNumb;
1989                    
1990                    cxStructs = orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports, txnSeqNumb);
1991            }
1992            else
1993            {
1994                    cxStructs = orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports, txnSeqNumb);
1995            }
1996            
1997        if ( ( isLightOrder() && getMyHome().shouldPublishCxlReportForLightOrder(cancelReason) ) || 
1998                        ( !isLightOrder() && getOrderOriginType() != InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER && !isLinkedAwayOrder() && !isLegDerivedOrder() ) )
1999        {
2000            if(os == null && !updateTXNSqNumb) //Direct publish so we need to initialize os for publishing here.
2001            {
2002                os = this.getOrderStruct();
2003            }
2004            
2005            getMyHome().getExtOrderStatusPublisher().acceptCancelReport(this.getRoutingStruct().groups,  StatusUpdateReasons.NEW,
2006                    os, reports, "");
2007        }
2008 
2009        MarketDetailStruct[] ohdStructs_emptyStruct = new MarketDetailStruct[0];
2010        
2011        
2012        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptCancelReport.getEventType()).acceptCancelReport(
2013                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(),
2014                getOrderId(), OrderStates.CANCEL,
2015                orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports), getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
2016                ohdStructs_emptyStruct, activityTime); 
2017        if (!isLightOrder() && (hadNBBOProtection() && cancelReason == ActivityReasons.USER) || needsDropCopyForLinkageOrders(reports[0].cancelReportType) || isMarkedForDropCopy())
2018        {
2019            getMyHome().publishIntermarketCancelReports(this, reports, cancelRequestId);
2020        }        
2021      
2022    }

2025                    long cancelRequestId, boolean updateTXNSqNumb, MarketDetailStruct[] ohdStructs)
2026    {
2027        //MarketDetailStruct[] ohdStructs =  buildMarketDetailStructs();
2028        int txnSeqNumb = getTransactionSequenceNumber();

2030            CancelStruct[] cxStructs = null;
2031            if(updateTXNSqNumb)
2032            {

2035            {
2036                 reports[i].transactionSequenceNumber = txnSeqNumb;
2037            }                
2038                    cxStructs = orderCancel.getCancelsFromCancelReports(reports, txnSeqNumb);

2142    
2143    final CancelReportStruct[] cancelLegs(CancelReportStruct spreadCxlRpt)
2144    throws DataValidationException
2145    {
2146            ProductStaticInfo spreadInfo = null;
2147            
2148            try
2149            {
2150                    spreadInfo = ((TradingProductImpl)getTradingProduct()).getProdInfo();
2151            }
2152            catch(Exception e)
2153            {
2154                    Log.exception("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this, e);
2155                       return new CancelReportStruct[] {spreadCxlRpt};
2156            }
2157                   CancelReportStruct[] reports = new CancelReportStruct[spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs.length+1];
2158                   reports[0] = spreadCxlRpt;
2159            try
2160               {                       
2161                       // in order to support buy/write, need to blindly get productKey from strategy impl...
2162                       for (int i = 0; i < reports.length-1; i++)
2163                       {
2164                               reports[i + 1] = cancelLeg(spreadCxlRpt.cancelReason,
2165                                               spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key,
2166                                               spreadCxlRpt.cancelledQuantity * spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legRatioQuantity,
2167                                               spreadCxlRpt.userAssignedCancelId);
2168                       }
2169                       return reports;
2170               }
2171               catch (Exception e)
2172               {
2173                       Log.exception("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this, e);
2174                       return reports;
2175                       //throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Failed to cancel legs for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
2176               }
2177    }

2235        report.executingOrGiveUpFirm = getExecutingOrGiveUpFirmStruct();
2236        report.extensions = extensions;
2237        report.fillReportType = ReportTypes.FILL_REJECT;
2238        report.leavesQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
2239        report.optionalData = getOptionalData();
2240        report.originator = getOriginatorAcronym(false);
2241        report.orsId = getOrsId();
2242        report.positionEffect = getPositionEffect();

2249                .getCurrentDateTimeInMillis());
2250        report.tradedQuantity = totalQuantity;
2251        report.tradeId = CboeId.toStruct(tradeId);

2261    /**
2262     * This method is to reject a fill for OUTGOING Linkage Order.
2263     *
2264     * @param tradedQuantity
2265     * @param tradePrice
2266     * @param fillReportExtensions
2267     * @param rejectReason
2268     */
2269    public void rejectFill(int tradedQuantity, PriceStruct tradePrice, String fillReportExtensions, short rejectReason) throws DataValidationException
2270    {
2271        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2272        {
2273            Log.debug(this, "request to reject the fill for order:" + getOrderIdString());
2274        }
2275 
2276        try
2277        {
2278            ExtensionsHelper helper = new ExtensionsHelper(fillReportExtensions);
2279            String awayExchangeExecId = helper.getValue(ExtensionFields.AWAY_EXCHANGE_EXEC_ID);
2280            //if( awayExchangeExecId == null  || awayExchangeExecId.equals(EMPTY_STRING) || execTime == null || execTime.equals(EMPTY_STRING))
2281            if (awayExchangeExecId == null || awayExchangeExecId.equals(EMPTY_STRING))
2282            {
2283                Log.information("Invalid request to rejectFill for order id: " + getOrderIdString());
2284                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Reject fill must have away exchange exec id and execution receipt time", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TIME);
2285            }
2286 
2287            //iF rejection is because of stale execution then send the original order time also.
2288            if (rejectReason == ActivityReasons.STALE_EXECUTION)
2289            {
2290                DateWrapper date = new DateWrapper(getOHSReceivedTime());
2291                helper.setValue(ExtensionFields.ORIGINAL_ORDER_TIME, date.format(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME));
2292 
2293                fillReportExtensions = helper.toString();
2294            }
2295        }
2296        catch (java.text.ParseException e)
2297        {
2298            Log.exception(this, "Parse exception while parsing the reject fill for order " + getOrderIdString(), e);
2299        }
2300        catch (FormatNotFoundException e)
2301        {
2302            Log.exception(this, "Date Parse exception while parsing the reject fill for order " + getOrderIdString(), e);
2303        }
2304        FilledReportStruct fillReject = buildReportForRejectFill(tradedQuantity, tradePrice, fillReportExtensions, rejectReason);
2305        FilledReportStruct[] fillRejectStructs = new FilledReportStruct[1];
2306        fillRejectStructs[0] = fillReject;
2307        publishFilledReports(fillRejectStructs, false, true, null, false,false); // this is rejected by External
2308    }

2312     *

2318private FilledReportStruct buildReportForRejectFill(int tradedQuantity, PriceStruct tradePrice, String fillReportExtensions, short rejectReason)

2330    report.orsId = getOrsId();

2335    report.side = getSideValue();
2336    report.subaccount = getSubAccount();

2356    }

2359    report.tradedQuantity = tradedQuantity;
2360    report.price = tradePrice;
2361

2418   public synchronized void updateForAsyncCreateTrade(int productKey, int tradedQuantity, Price tradePrice) throws DataValidationException
2419   {
2420           if (Log.isDebugOn())
2421                {
2422                        Log.debug("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >> updating tradable orderId = " + getOrderIdString() + " productKey = " + productKey + ", tradedQuantity = " + tradedQuantity + ", tradePrice = " + tradePrice + " for ASYNC_TRADE");
2423                }
2424        
2425           if (productKey == getPrimitiveProductKey()) //case for simple options and/or strategy orders. Doesn't take care of legs, see else clause below.
2426       {
2427               try
2428           {
2429                   checkTradedQuantity(tradedQuantity);
2430 
2431                            HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
2432                            if (handlingInstruction != null)
2433                            {
2434                                    int totalTraded = handlingInstruction.getTradedVolume() + tradedQuantity;
2435                                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
2436                                    {
2437                                            Log.debug("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >>  for [orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + "] for ASYNC_TRADE - handlingInstruction traded volume set to: " + totalTraded);
2438                                    }
2439                                    handlingInstruction.setTradedVolume(totalTraded);
2440                                    if ( ! handlingInstruction.isDefaultMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid())
2441                                    {
2442                                            handlingInstruction.setMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid(
2443                                                            handlingInstruction.getMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid() - tradedQuantity);
2444                                    }
2445                            }
2446 
2447                   setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() + tradedQuantity);
2448 
2449                   if (getInitialTradePrice() == null)
2450                   {
2451                           setInitialTradePrice(tradePrice);
2452                   }
2453 
2454                   if (getRemainingQuantity() == 0)
2455                   {
2456                           setState(OrderStates.FILL);
2457                   }
2458 
2459                   if(tradePrice.isValuedPrice())
2460                   {
2461                           adjustTotalPrice(tradedQuantity, tradePrice.toDouble());
2462                   }
2463                   else 
2464                   {
2465                           adjustTotalPrice(tradedQuantity, 0.0);
2466                   }
2467 
2468                   adjustTotalSessionTradedQuantity(tradedQuantity);
2469                   asyncCreateTradePending++;
2470                   if (Log.isDebugOn())
2471           {
2472                       Log.debug("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >> asyncCreateTradePending incremented to " + asyncCreateTradePending + " for [orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + "] for ASYNC_TRADE");
2473                   }
2474               }
2475               catch(DataValidationException dve)
2476               {
2477                   Log.alarm("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >> got DataValidationException for orderId = " + getOrderIdString() + " productKey = " + productKey + ", tradedQuantity = " + tradedQuantity + " must be quantity mismatch - for ASYNC_TRADE " + dve);
2478               }
2479       }
2480           else // case for strategy's legs only. The strategy order itself is taken care of in the if clause above.
2481           {
2482               LegOrderDetail legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(productKey);
2483                int remainingQuantity = legDetail.getLeavesQuantity();
2484                if (tradedQuantity > remainingQuantity)  {
2485                    Log.alarm("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >> Order [" + legDetail.getOrderIdString() + "] got a fill request for " + tradedQuantity + " contracts; it only has " + remainingQuantity + " available - for ASYNC_TRADE");
2486                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("OrderImpl::updateForAsyncCreateTrade >> Traded quantity is greater than remaining quantity of the order", 0);
2487                }        
2488                legDetail.setTradedQuantity(legDetail.getTradedQuantity() + tradedQuantity);
2489           }
2490       //asyncCreateTradePending++;
2491           
2492    }
2493 
2494        /**
2495         * carry out the task to fill the order and return a filled report struct
2496         */
2497   private FilledReportStruct doOrderFill(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String executingBroker, char billingType, boolean updateTradable, TradableSnapShot captuerdFillData)
2498            throws DataValidationException
2499    {
2500       if (Log.isDebugOn())
2501       {
2502           Log.debug("OrderImpl::doOrderFill >> invoqued [orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + "] tradeId = " + tradeId + ", productKey = " + productKey +
2503                   " fill(quantity=" + totalQuantity + ", tradePrice=" + tradePrice.toDouble() +
2504                   ", contraParties[" + (contraParties == null ? "null array" : "" + contraParties.length) + "]), updateTradable = " + updateTradable +
2505                   " - for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE. CaptuerdFillData: \n" + (captuerdFillData == null ? "null" : "" + captuerdFillData));
2506       }
2507       FilledReportStruct report = null;
2508 
2509       if(updateTradable)
2510                {
2511            checkTradedQuantity(totalQuantity);
2512        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
2513        if (handlingInstruction != null)
2514        {
2515                int totalTraded = handlingInstruction.getTradedVolume() + totalQuantity;
2516                handlingInstruction.setTradedVolume(totalTraded);
2517                                if ( ! handlingInstruction.isDefaultMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid())
2518                                {
2519                    handlingInstruction.setMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid(
2520                            handlingInstruction.getMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid() - totalQuantity);
2521                }
2522                    }
2523                    setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() + totalQuantity);
2524 
2525        if (getInitialTradePrice() == null)
2526        {
2527                setInitialTradePrice(tradePrice);
2528            }
2529                }
2530 
2531                report = buildFilledReportStruct(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties, executingBroker, billingType, captuerdFillData);
2532                
2533                //Added for CFLEX 2.0 - Pending Trades.
2534                try
2535            {
2536                if(getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().isFlexStrategyProduct(getTradingProduct()) || tradePrice.isPercentagePrice())
2537                {
2538                         addFillReportToList(report);
2539                }
2540            }
2541            catch (NotFoundException ex)
2542            {
2543                Log.exception(this, "No product found with key = " + getProductKey(), ex);                
2544            }
2545                if (Log.isDebugOn())
2546                {
2547           Log.debug("OrderImpl::doOrderFill >> Order " + getOrderIdString() + "  with tradeId = " + tradeId + ", productKey = " + productKey + " got filled for " + totalQuantity + " contracts for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE");
2548                }
2549 
2550                if (getRemainingQuantity() == 0)
2551                {
2552           if(updateTradable)
2553                setState(OrderStates.FILL);
2554            }
2555        
2556        // store filled report for cross product leg trading and spread to leg trade from STS
2557        try
2558        {
2559            if(isCrossProductLegOrder())
2560        {
2561            addFillReportToList(report);
2562 
2563            ExtensionsHelper helper = getExtensionsHelper(report.extensions, "for fill report");
2564            addValueToExtensionsHelper(helper, "" + FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.TAGNUMBER, FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.CBOE);
2565            report.extensions = helper.toString();
2566            }
2567            else if(isStrategy() && isRolledoutSpreadClass() && getTradingProduct().isProxy())
2568            {
2569                addFillReportToList(report);
2570            }
2571            
2572            
2573        }
2574        catch (NotFoundException e)
2575        {
2576            Log.alarm("TradingProduct is not found for product: " + this.productKey);
2577        }    
2578        
2579       if (Log.isDebugOn())
2580       {
2581           Log.debug("OrderImpl::doOrderFill >> about to return filledReportStruct " + getOrderIdString() + " for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE, filledReportStruct: \n" +
2582                     " tradeId = " + tradeId + " orsId = " + report.orsId + ", orderId = " + getOrderIdString() + ", fillReportType = " + report.fillReportType + 
2583                     ", productKey = " + report.productKey + ", sessionName = " + report.sessionName + ", tradedQuantity = " + report.tradedQuantity +
2584                     ", leavesQuantity = " + report.leavesQuantity + ", price type= " + report.price.type + ", price= " + report.price.whole + "." + report.price.fraction +
2585                     ", side = " + report.side + ", contraParties[" + (contraParties == null ? "null array" : "" + contraParties.length)+ "]" +
2586                     ", positionEffect = " + positionEffect + ", executingBroker = " + report.executingBroker
2587           );
2588       }
2589       
2590            return report;
2591        }

2629        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2630        {
2631            Log.debug("OrderImpl::doLegFill >> invoqued [orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + "] with tradeID = " + tradeId + " fill(quantity=" + totalQuantity + ", tradePrice=" + tradePrice.toDouble() + ", contraParties[" + (contraParties == null ? "null array" : "" + contraParties.length) + "]) - for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE");
2632        }        
2633        FilledReportStruct report = null;
2634        try
2635        {
2636            LegOrderDetail legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(productKey);
2637            report = legDetail.fill(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties, updateTradable, captuerdFillData);
2638            
2639            BillingStrategy.setBillingType(report, billingType);
2640            BillingStrategy.setBillingType(report, billingType);
2641            populateCommonValueForReport(report, executingBroker);
2642            populateSpecialvalues(report, productKey);
2643            if(isStrategy() && isRolledoutSpreadClass() && getTradingProduct().isProxy())
2644            {
2645                addFillReportToList(report);
2646            }
2647            //Added for CFLEX 2.0 - Pending Trades.
2648            try
2649            {
2650                if(getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().isFlexStrategyProduct(getTradingProduct()) || tradePrice.isPercentagePrice())
2651                {
2652                     addFillReportToList(report);
2653                }
2654            }
2655            catch (NotFoundException ex)
2656            {
2657                Log.exception(this, "No product found with key = " + getProductKey(), ex);                
2658            }
2659        }
2660        catch (Exception e)
2661        {
2662                        Log.exception("not found the leg with product key = " + productKey + " of strategy " + getPrimitiveProductKey(), e);
2663                }
2664        if (Log.isDebugOn())
2665        {
2666            Log.debug("OrderImpl::doOrderFill >> about to return filledReportStruct " + getOrderIdString() + " for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE, filledReportStruct: \n" +
2667                      " tradeId = " + tradeId + " orsId = " + report.orsId + ", orderId = " + getOrderIdString() + ", fillReportType = " + report.fillReportType + 
2668                      ", productKey = " + report.productKey + ", sessionName = " + report.sessionName + ", tradedQuantity = " + report.tradedQuantity +
2669                      ", leavesQuantity = " + report.leavesQuantity + ", price = " + report.price.toString() + 
2670                      ", side = " + report.side + ", contraParties[" + (contraParties == null ? "null array" : "" + contraParties.length)+ "]" +
2671                      ", positionEffect = " + positionEffect + ", executingBroker = " + report.executingBroker
2672            );
2673        }  
2674                return report;
2675        }

2677    private String getSessionNameForProduct(int productKey)
2678    {
2679        String sessionName = null;
2680        try
2681        {
2682            int classKey = getMyHome().getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(productKey).getProductKeysStruct().classKey;
2683            sessionName =  getMyHome().getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductClassData(classKey).getSessionNames()[0];
2684        }
2685        catch (Exception e)
2686        {
2687            Log.exception(this, "Cannot get sessionName for the leg of outside tradeEngine, for prodKey= "
2688                    + productKey, e);
2689        }
2690        return sessionName;
2691    }
2692    /**
2693     * This menthod is to fill  special fields for FIX usage (requested by FIX, Trade OPS requirement)
2694     * to indicate this leg fill is sent from SecurityExchange CBOE (W)
2695     * Here it is hard coded with constant W, apply to stock leg fill report
2696     * filled in W_MAIN (option) only.

2698     * @param productKey

2700    private void populateSpecialvalues(FilledReportStruct report, int productKey)

2703                && !getSessionNameForProduct(productKey).equals(getActiveSession()))
2704        {

2706            addValueToExtensionsHelper(helper, "" + FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.TAGNUMBER, FixUtilConstants.SecurityExchange.CBOE);
2707            report.extensions = helper.toString();
2708        }
2709    }

2716        private FilledReportStruct buildFilledReportStruct(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, short tradeContext, char billingType)
2717        {

2721        /**
2722         * build the filled report struct based on the informtion supplied
2723         * to calculate leaves quantity, use the method getRemainingQuantityForFillReport
2724         * UD 03/07/04 ...
2725         */
2726    private FilledReportStruct buildFilledReportStruct(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String executingBroker, char billingType, TradableSnapShot captuerdFillData)
2727    {
2728            FilledReportStruct report = new FilledReportStruct();
2729            report.fillReportType = getFillReportType();
2730            report.tradeId = CboeId.toStruct(tradeId);
2731            report.productKey = productKey;
2732            report.tradedQuantity = totalQuantity;
2733            report.leavesQuantity = getRemainingQuantityForFillReport();
2734            
2735            if(captuerdFillData != null)
2736            {
2737                    report.leavesQuantity = captuerdFillData.getRemainingFillVoume();
2738            }
2739            //report.leavesQuantity = totalQuantity - getOriginalQuantity(true);
2740            report.price = adjustPriceForReport(tradePrice).toStruct();
2741            report.contraParties = contraParties;
2742            report.positionEffect = getPositionEffect();
2743            report.side = getSideValue();
2744            populateCommonValueForReport(report, executingBroker);
2745            BillingStrategy.setBillingType(report, billingType);
2746            return report;
2747        }
2748 
2749        /**
2750         * The trade price in the system will always be the price for the asDefinedSide
2751         * if the product is strategy. But when reporting the price to the user when order
2752         * gets filled, the sign of the price has to be adjusted according. That is:
2753         * if the side of the order is OppositeSide, then sign of the price reported to
2754         * user should be flipped
2755         */
2756    private Price adjustPriceForReport(Price tradePrice)
2757    {
2758       // if (isOppositeSide() && tradePrice.isValuedPrice())
2759            if(isOppositeSide())
2760        {
2761                    if(tradePrice.isValuedPrice())
2762                    {
2763                            return PriceFactory.createValuedPrice (-1 * tradePrice.toDouble());
2764                    }
2765                    else if(tradePrice.isPercentagePrice())
2766                    {
2767                            return PriceFactory.createPercentagePrice (-1 * tradePrice.toDouble());
2768                    }
2769            
2770        }
2771        return tradePrice;
2772   }

2774        /**
2775         * determine the report type
2776         * 
2777         * Modified for CFLEX 2.0 - Pending Trades
2778         */
2779    public short getReportType()
2780    {
2781        try
2782        {
2783            if (getTradingProduct().isStrategy())
2784            {
2785                return ReportTypes.STRATEGY_REPORT;
2786            }
2787        }
2788        catch (Exception e)
2789        {
2790            Log.exception(e);
2791        }
2792        return ReportTypes.REGULAR_REPORT;
2793    }
2794 
2795    /**
2796     * determine the report type
2797     * 
2798     * Modified for CFLEX 2.0 - Pending Trades
2799     */
2800    public short getFillReportType()
2801    {
2802        try
2803        {
2804            if (getTradingProduct().isStrategy())
2805            {
2806                if(getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().isFlexStrategyProduct(getTradingProduct()))
2807                {
2808                    if(getPrice().isPercentagePrice())
2809                    {
2810                        return  ReportTypes.PENDING_PRICE;
2811                    }
2812                    return ReportTypes.PENDING_LEG_PRICE;
2813                }
2814                return ReportTypes.STRATEGY_REPORT;
2815            }
2816            else
2817            {
2818                if(getPrice().isPercentagePrice())
2819                {
2820                    return ReportTypes.PENDING_PRICE;
2821                }
2822            }
2823        }
2824        catch (Exception e)
2825        {
2826            Log.exception(e);
2827        }
2828        return ReportTypes.REGULAR_REPORT;
2829    }

2834    {

2837        report.userAcronym = getUserAcronym();

2840        report.account = getAccount();
2841        report.subaccount = getSubAccount();
2842        report.originator = getOriginatorAcronym(false);
2843        report.optionalData = getOptionalData();
2844        report.userAssignedId = getUserAssignedId();
2845        //report.extensions = getExtensions(); //-MW  probably, people desided just leave it empty 07/22/2002
2846        if (report.extensions == null)
2847        {
2848            report.extensions = "";
2849        }
2850        report.timeSent = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(new java.util.Date().getTime());
2851        report.executingOrGiveUpFirm = getClearingFirm();
2852        report.sessionName = getActiveSession();
2853        report.executingBroker = executingBroker;
2854        if (isICMOrder())
2855        {
2856            overrideFillReportWithProfile(report);
2857        }
2858        else if (clearsLikeQuote())
2859        {
2860                if ((getAccount() == null) || (getAccount().length() == 0))
2861                {
2862                    // just use the accout from profile then.
2863                    overrideFillReportWithProfile(report);
2864                }
2865        }
2866    }

2868        /**
2869         * return true if all legs' remaining quantity is zero. If this is a regular order, it
2870         * always return false(because there is no leg for regular order).
2871         */
2872    public boolean legsHaveRemainingQuantity()
2873    {
2874        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
2875        for (int i = 0; i < legs.length; i++)
2876        {
2877            if (legs[i].getLeavesQuantity() != 0)
2878            {
2879                return true;
2880            }
2881        }
2882        return false;
2883    }

3064    /**
3065     * Publish the FilledReports
3066     */
3067    public void publishFilledReports(FilledReportStruct[] reports, boolean internalFills, boolean publishReport, TradableSnapShot fillSnapShot, boolean updateTradable, boolean asyncCall)
3068    {
3069    // UD 10/08/04...
3070    // In QuoteTrigger condition, order's remaningQty doesn't match filled report
3071    // remaningQty on a parital fill, so need to calculate remaining qty of the order
3072    // as done for the filledOrderStruct.leavesQuantity ...
3073      
3074            boolean ayncPublishFill = (isAsyncCreateTradePending() && updateTradable);
3075            
3076            if (Log.isDebugOn())
3077        {
3078            Log.debug(this, "OrderImpl::publishFilledReports>>" + getOrderIdString() +">> AsyncCreateTradePending=" + asyncCreateTradePending + ", updateTradable=" + updateTradable + ", asyncCall=" + asyncCall);
3079        }
3080            
3081            if(!ayncPublishFill)
3082                {
3083                    incrementSequenceNumber();
3084                }
3085            
3086            for (FilledReportStruct fillReport : reports)
3087            {
3088                    fillReport.transactionSequenceNumber = getTransactionSequenceNumber();
3089            }
3090             
3091            if(publishReport) 
3092            {
3093                
3094                    if(fillSnapShot == null)
3095                    {
3096        applyFillOnTheOrder(reports);
3097                    }
3098 
3099                        OrderStruct os = this.getOrderStruct();        
3100                        if(fillSnapShot != null)
3101                        {
3102                                os.state = fillSnapShot.getTradableState();
3103                                os.cancelledQuantity = fillSnapShot.getCanceledTotalVolume();

3113        if (!(getOrderOriginType() == InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER || isLinkedAwayOrder() || isLegDerivedOrder()))

3152                        }
3153                    }
3154                    else
3155                    {

3201            }
3202        }
3203        catch (Exception ex)
3204        {
3205            //Catching this exception here is a side effect of moving the recordOrderExecution to this method.
3206            //The publishIntermarketFilledReports has the same "catch-all" block so I had to keep the behavior
3207            //the same instead of propogating the exception.

3209        }
3210            }

3236                    case ActivityTypes.NEW_TRADE_PRICE : return true;

3642 
3643    /**
3644     * Return the part of the total quantity which is allowed to trade.
3645     * <p/>
3646     * Note: getQuantity() should return the total available quantity of a tradable.
3647     *      but in a particular trade, we may only want to trade with a partial of
3648     *      the total available quantity, which is specified by the result of getQuantityAllowable()
3649     */
3650    public int getQuantityAllowed()
3651    {
3652        if(!calculateQuantityAllowed)
3653        {
3654            //If this flag is set to false we just want to return back with 0 so that it cannot take part in trading.
3655            return 0;
3656        }
3657        // Check if Max AutoEx Quantity should be used. If MaxQuantity is set to default means, we never
3658        // touched it so skip any further logic.
3659        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
3660        if (handlingInstruction != null &&
3661            ! handlingInstruction.isDefaultMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid() )
3662        {
3663            int maxRemainingQuantity = handlingInstruction.getMaxTradableQtyForIndexHybrid();
3664            if (maxRemainingQuantity < getRemainingQuantityForTrade() ) 
3665            {
3666                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
3667                {
3668                    Log.debug("OrderImpl >>> getQuantityAllowed for orderId: " + getOrderIdString() +" and returning " + maxRemainingQuantity);
3669                }
3670                return maxRemainingQuantity;
3671            } 
3672        }
3673 
3674        return getRemainingQuantityForTrade();
3675    }

3687    /**
3688     * This method calculates the order's remaining quantity for Fill Report.
3689     * 03/08/04...
3690     * author Uma Diddi
3691     *
3692     * @return int
3693     */
3694    public int getRemainingQuantityForFillReport()
3695    {
3696        return getOriginalQuantity(true) +
3697                getAddedQuantity() -
3698                getTradedQuantity() -
3699                getCancelledQuantity();
3700    }
3701 
3702    /**
3703     * This method calculates the orders remaining quantity allowed for trade.
3704     * The remaining quantity for trade may differ from the actual remaining quantity
3705     * but should be less than or equal to the actual remaining quantity
3706     */
3707    public int getRemainingQuantityForTrade()
3708    {
3709            int remainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
3710        HandlingInstruction handlingInstruction = getHandlingInstruction();
3711        if (handlingInstruction == null)
3712        {
3713            return remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity() - getOddLotFlashedQuantity();
3714        }
3715 
3716        short tradingRestriction = handlingInstruction.getTradingRestriction();
3717        int allowedQ = 0;
3718        short handlingMode = handlingInstruction.getRemainderHandlingMode();
3719 
3720        // Because AIM is internalized order, maximumExecutionVolume is ignored; ship quantity is excluded for trade&ship
3721        if (handlingMode == RemainderHandlingModes.AUCTION_AND_RETURN_REMAINDER)
3722        {
3723            allowedQ = remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity();;
3724        }
3725        // for HAL order, maximumExecutionVolume is ignored; ship quantity is excluded for trade&ship
3726        else if (handlingMode == RemainderHandlingModes.HAL)
3727        {
3728            allowedQ = remainingQuantity - getShipQuantity();;
3729        }
3730        else if (tradingRestriction == TradingRestrictions.SWEEP_AND_RETURN)
3731        {
3732            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();;
3733        }
3734        else if (tradingRestriction == TradingRestrictions.FISH_AND_RETURN)
3735        {
3736            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();
3737        }
3738        else if (TradingRestrictions.NONE == tradingRestriction &&
3739                 handlingInstruction.getRemainderHandlingMode() == RemainderHandlingModes.RETURN_REMAINDER) {
3740            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity() - getShipQuantity();
3741        }
3742        else
3743        {
3744            allowedQ = handlingInstruction.getAllowedQuantity();
3745        }
3746 
3747        if (allowedQ >= remainingQuantity)
3748        {
3749                if (Log.isDebugOn())
3750            {
3751                Log.debug("OrderImpl >>> getRemainingQuantityForTrade for orderId: " + getOrderIdString() +" and returning " + remainingQuantity);
3752            }
3753            return remainingQuantity;
3754        }
3755        if (Log.isDebugOn())
3756        {
3757            Log.debug("OrderImpl >>> getRemainingQuantityForTradefor orderId: " + getOrderIdString() + " returning " + allowedQ);
3758        }
3759        return allowedQ;
3760    }
3761

3763{
3764        if(this.order_side != null){
3765        return order_side;
3766        }else
3767    {
3768        setOrderSide(getSideValue());
3769        return getOrderSide();  
3770    }

3959/**
3960 * convert the internal state to external state
3961 */
3962    private short getExternalOrderState()
3963    {
3964    if (getState() == OrderStates.ACTIVE ||
3965        getState() == InternalOrderStates.ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT ||
3966        getState() == InternalOrderStates.IPP_EXPOSING ||
3967        getState() == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY ||
3968        getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_WAITING ||
3969        getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_EXPOSING)
3970    {
3971        return OrderStates.BOOKED;
3972    }
3973    else if(getState() == InternalOrderStates.INACTIVE_CANCEL_RE_REQUEST_PENDING)
3974    {
3975        return OrderStates.INACTIVE;
3976    }
3977 
3978    return getState();
3979}

3990    return getOrderOriginType();

4046    /**
4047     * Checks to see if all legs have been cancelled.  Result will only be true if remaining quantity
4048     * is 0 on all legs and no leg has any traded quantity.
4049     */
4050    protected boolean allLegsCancelled()
4051    {
4052        boolean result = getProductType() == ProductTypes.STRATEGY;
4053        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
4054        for (int i = 0; result && i < legs.length; i++)
4055        {
4056            result = legs[i].getLeavesQuantity() == 0 && legs[i].getTradedQuantity() == 0;
4057        }
4058        return result;
4059    }
4060 
4061    /**
4062     * Checks to see if all legs have been filled.  Result will only be true if remaining quantity
4063     * is 0 on all legs and no leg has any cancelled quantity.
4064     */
4065    protected boolean allLegsFilled()
4066    {
4067        boolean result = getProductType() == ProductTypes.STRATEGY;
4068        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
4069        for (int i = 0; result && i < legs.length; i++)
4070        {
4071            result = legs[i].getLeavesQuantity() == 0 && legs[i].getCancelledQuantity() == 0;
4072        }
4073        return result;
4074    }

4079     * (for orders traded in SBT) are AON and FOK.
4080     */
4081    public boolean hasVolumeContingency()
4082    {

4084        {
4085            return false;
4086        }

4088    }

4151 
4152public boolean isAuctionActive()
4153{
4154    boolean beingAuctioned = false;
4155    try
4156    {
4157        TradingProduct product = getTradingProduct();
4158        AuctionInternal auction  = product.getActiveAuction();
4159        if (auction != null)
4160        {
4161            Order auctionedOrder = null;
4162            AuctionBook auctionBook = auction.getAuctionBook();
4163            if(auctionBook != null)
4164            {
4165                     auctionedOrder = auctionBook.getAuctionedOrder();
4166            }
4167            else
4168            {
4169                    auctionedOrder = auction.getAuctionedOrder();
4170            }
4171            if (auctionedOrder == null)
4172            {
4173                return false;
4174            }
4175            long auctionedOrderId = auctionedOrder.getUniqueId();
4176            if (auctionedOrderId == this.getUniqueId())
4177            {
4178                beingAuctioned = true;
4179            }  
4180        }
4181    }
4182    catch (NotFoundException nfe)
4183    {
4184        beingAuctioned = false;
4185    }
4186    return beingAuctioned;
4187}

4189/**
4190 * Determins if this order can be reinstated after a bust
4191     *
4192 * @return boolean
4193 */
4194public boolean isReinstatable()
4195{
4196    if (isMinSizeGuaranteeOrder() || treatedLikeQuote() || isAuctionActive()) {
4197 
4198        return false;
4199    }
4200    short contingencyType = getContingencyType();
4201    if (contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.CLOSE ||
4202            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP ||
4203            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.OPG) {
4204        return true;
4205    }
4206    if (contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.NONE ||
4207            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.AON ||
4208            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.RESERVE ||
4209            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP_LOSS ||
4210            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.STP_LIMIT || 
4211            contingencyType == com.cboe.idl.cmiConstants.ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP_BOOK)
4212        {
4213            if (!getPrice().isMarketPrice())
4214            {
4215            return true;
4216        }
4217    }
4218    return false;
4219}

4256    public static String orderIdToString(OrderIdStruct orderId)
4257{
4258    String result;
4259        if (orderId.highCboeId != 0)
4260        {
4261        result = orderId.highCboeId + ":" + orderId.lowCboeId;
4262    }
4263        else
4264        {
4265        String orderDate = "";
4266        try
4267        {
4268                orderDate = orderId.orderDate.equals("") ? (new DateWrapper()).format("OrderDate") : orderId.orderDate;
4269        }
4270            catch (com.cboe.util.FormatNotFoundException e)
4271        {
4272            Log.alarm("orderIdToString: No OrderDate available for order :" +
4273                orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange + ":" +
4274                orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber + ":" +
4275                orderId.branch + ":" +
4276                orderId.branchSequenceNumber + ":" +
4277                orderId.correspondentFirm
4278                );
4279        }
4280        result =  orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange + ":" +
4281            orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber + ":" +
4282            orderId.branch + ":" +
4283            orderId.branchSequenceNumber + ":" +
4284            orderId.correspondentFirm + ":" +
4285            orderDate;
4286    }
4287    return result;
4288}

4392    /**
4393    *  Will reinstate the quantity specified.  This has the net effect of increasing remaining quantity by the specified quantity.
4394     *
4395    *  @param quantity  The quantity to reinstate
4396     * @throws DataValidationException if quantity > bustedQuantity
4397    */
4398    public void reinstate(long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
4399    {
4400        if (quantity > getBustedQuantity())
4401        {
4402            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot reinstate more quantity than is busted",
4403                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
4404        }
4405        if (getState() == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY)
4406        {
4407            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot reinstate the order being at OMT/PAR/OHS.",
4408                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_ORDER_STATE);
4409        }
4410        if (!isActive())
4411        {
4412            setState(OrderStates.ACTIVE);
4413        }
4414        //Reduced busted quantity by the specified quantity, this will in effect raise remaining quantity.
4415        //setBustedQuantity(getBustedQuantity() - quantity);
4416        setCancelledQuantity(getCancelledQuantity() - quantity);
4417        if (propagateToOrderLegs())
4418        {
4419            reinstateLegs(quantity);
4420        }
4421 
4422                //Increase the sequence number before create history to avoid the duplicated order id in history
4423                incrementSequenceNumber();
4424        getMyHome().addOrderToCache(this);
4425        publishBustReinstateReport(tradeId, quantity);
4426    }
4427 
4428    /**
4429     * Updates the legs with the reinstated quantity.
4430     */
4431    private void reinstateLegs(int quantity) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
4432    {
4433            try
4434            {
4435                    ProductStaticInfo spreadInfo = ((TradingProductImpl)getTradingProduct()).getProdInfo();
4436                    for (int i = 0; i < spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs.length; ++i)
4437                    {
4438                            try
4439                            {
4440                                    // in order to support buy/write, need to blindly get productKey from strategy impl...
4441                                    LegOrderDetail legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key);
4442                                    legDetail.reinstate(quantity * spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legRatioQuantity);
4443                            }
4444                            catch (Exception e)
4445                            {
4446                                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Unable to reinstate on leg of prod["+spreadInfo.spreadParams.legs[i].legProd.key+"] for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
4447                            }
4448                    }
4449            }
4450            catch (NotFoundException e)
4451            {
4452                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Unable to reinstate for order::"+this+"::"+e.getMessage(), 0);
4453        }
4454    }
4455

4557    /**

4569                || isBookingOddLot() && treatedLikeQuote() || isPartOfCross())
4570        {

4573        else
4574        {
4575            return true;
4576        }
4577    }

4589    private int getIPPMinSize()
4590    {

4595            result = tradingClass.getTradingPropertyIPPMinSize();
4596        }
4597        catch (NotFoundException e)
4598        {

4600        }

4602    }
