4604    /**
4605    * Tells the tradable can now book itself if it OKs it
4606     * <p/>
4607    * author Connie Liang
4608    */
4609    public void handleBookProcessing(OrderBook book) throws DataValidationException
4610    {
4611            boolean booked = isBooked();
4612            if (booked)
4613            {
4614                    try
4615                    {
4616                       int qtyToUpdate = getQuantityAllowed()-getBookedQuantity();
4617                       if (qtyToUpdate!=0)
4618                            book.update(this, qtyToUpdate, true);
4619                    }
4620                    catch (Exception e)
4621                    {
4622                            Log.alarm("failed to find the booked order for update, just add it in: "+this);
4623                            resetBookedTime();
4624                            booked = false;
4625                    }
4626            }
4627            if (!booked && eligibleForBook()) {
4628            prevReservedQuantity=0;
4629            prevDisplayedQuantity = 0;
4630            prevRemainingQuantity=0;
4631            displayQuantity=0;
4632            book.acceptTradable(this);
4633        } else {
4634            postBookUpdateProcessing(this, null);
4635        }
4636    }
4637    /**
4638     *
4639     */
4640    public void postBookUpdateProcessing(OrderBook book)
4641        throws DataValidationException
4642    {
4643        postBookUpdateProcessing( this, book );
4644    }
4645 
4646    /**
4647    * Tells the tradable can now start to process its own logic
4648    * after the book is updated.
4649    *
4650    * @param Order is passed because there may be a DerivedOrder wrapping
4651    * this order in which case we need to unbook that one
4652    *
4653    * author Connie Liang
4654    */
4655    public void postBookUpdateProcessing(Order self, OrderBook book)
4656    throws DataValidationException
4657    {
4658        int myquantity = getQuantityAllowed();
4659 
4660         
4661        if( isBookingOddLot() && treatedLikeQuote() )    
4662        {
4663            //When an order is Q-like, then we cancel when only an odd lot remains. 
4664                if (isBooked())
4665               unbookOrder(self, book, myquantity);
4666            cancel(ActivityReasons.INSUFFICIENT_QUANTITY);
4667        }
4668        else if( !eligibleForBook()   && myquantity != 0 && !isPartOfCross())
4669        {
4670 
4671            //Although when the order has been assigned to the NBBO Agent it is no longer
4672            //eligible for booking; however, in this case we won't want to cancel the order.
4673            
4674            String cancelStrategy = getBelowIPPMinSizeProcessingStrategy();
4675 
4676            if(cancelStrategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.CANCEL_ORDER_BELOW_IPP))
4677            {
4678                if(Log.isDebugOn())
4679                {
4680                    Log.debug(this, "Insufficient quantity. Need to cancel the order...");
4681                }
4682                if (isBooked())
4683                   unbookOrder(self, book, myquantity);
4684                cancel(ActivityReasons.INSUFFICIENT_QUANTITY);
4685            }
4686            else
4687            {
4688                // ??? Hmm, what about booking since the cancel strategy is not CANCEL_ORDER_BELOW_IPP
4689            }
4690        }
4691        else if( getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE && myquantity > 0 )
4692        {
4693            if( hasReserveQuantityDisplayed )
4694            {
4695                hasReserveQuantityDisplayed = false;
4696                // Keep the original state of the order before rebooking.
4697                short originalState = self.getState();
4698                
4699                // Rebook the order to make it lose priority.
4700            
4701                rebookOrder(self, book, myquantity );
4702                
4703                // The rebook is causing some orders to not be sent to autolink,
4704                // (when the displayQty was filled during the trade) 
4705                // To fix this, set the state of the order to the original state
4706                // before rebooking (IPP_EXPOSING), this way it will 
4707                // be sent to autolink.
4708                // (PITS 11751)
4709                if (self.isTradable(TradableTypes.NBBO_DERIVED_ORDER) &&
4710                    originalState == InternalOrderStates.IPP_EXPOSING)
4711                {
4712                    self.changeToState(originalState);
4713                }
4714            }
4715        }
4716        // if IOC I order then check below logic
4717        // check if the tradable is still either market against other side book,
4718        // or opposite auction price
4719        cancelIOCQuoteLikeOrder(self, true, book);
4720    }
4721 
4722    private boolean unbookOrder(Order self, OrderBook book, int cancelQuantity)
4723    {       
4724        if (cancelQuantity == 0)
4725                return false;
4726        
4727        //The book does not know about any odd lot portions for quote like orders
4728        if(book == null )
4729        {
4730            return false;
4731        }
4732 
4733        try
4734        {
4735            book.unbook(self, cancelQuantity, self.getSide(), self.getLastBookedPrice());
4736            return true;
4737        }
4738        catch(Exception e)
4739        {
4740            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when unbook the Order: " + e.toString());
4741            return false;
4742        }
4743    }
4744 
4745    /**
4746     * Rebook the order in the order book so that it loses priority
4747     */
4748    private void rebookOrder(Order self, OrderBook book, int quantity )
4749    {
4750        if(book == null)
4751        {
4752            return;
4753        }
4754 
4755        try
4756        {
4757                if (self.isBooked())
4758                {
4759               book.unbook(self, quantity, self.getSide(), self.getLastBookedPrice());
4760                }
4761        }
4762        catch(Exception e)
4763        {
4764            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when rebook::unbook the Order::"+self+" -- "+e.toString());
4765        }
4766        prevRemainingQuantity = 0;
4767        prevReservedQuantity = 0;
4768        prevDisplayedQuantity = 0;
4769        displayQuantity = 0;
4770 
4771        try
4772        {
4773            book.acceptTradable(self);
4774        }
4775        catch(Exception e)
4776        {
4777            Log.alarm(this, "exception occurred when rebook::rebook the Order::"+self+" -- "+e.toString());
4778        }
4779    }

4824 * ACCT (Account data)

4829    public void update(OrderHandlingStruct newValues)

4838         *  and the validation is far earlier in the process.

4845        if (newQty>curQty)

4847        else if (newQty<curQty)
4848                setCancelledQuantity(getCancelledQuantity()+curQty-newQty);
4849        */
4850        LegOrderDetailStruct[] newLegDetails = newValues.legOrderDetails;

4854            {

4892    /**
4893     * Checks to see if the account need to be blanked.  For ALLSESSIONS profile,
4894     * we need to check if the xml configuration for the session is set.  Otherwise, use the
4895     * flag set in the profile for the user.
4896     *
4897     * @param profileStruct
4898     * @param currentAccount
4899     * @param userAcronym
4900     */
4901    private String checkBlankAccount(SessionProfileStruct profileStruct, String currentAccount, String userAcronym)
4902    {
4903        String account = currentAccount;
4904        boolean isAllSessions = SessionProfileHelper.isProfileForAllSessions(profileStruct);
4905        if (userAcronym.equalsIgnoreCase(currentAccount) && !isAllSessions && profileStruct.isAccountBlanked)
4906        {
4907            // we want to send blank account, when the flag is ON
4908            account = EMPTY_STRING;
4909            if (Log.isDebugOn())
4910            {
4911                Log.debug("Want to send blank account, when the profile flag is ON, for userAcronym: "
4912                                + userAcronym + " using profile:(" + profileStruct.sessionName + ":" + profileStruct.classKey + ":"
4913                                + profileStruct.account + ":" + profileStruct.subAccount + ":"
4914                                + profileStruct.executingGiveupFirm.exchange + "-" + profileStruct.executingGiveupFirm.firmNumber + ":"
4915                                + profileStruct.isAccountBlanked + ")");
4916            }
4917        }
4918        else if (isAllSessions && userAcronym.equalsIgnoreCase(currentAccount)
4919            && getMyHome().blankAccountIfSameAsAcr())
4920        {
4921            if (Log.isDebugOn())
4922            {
4923            Log.debug(this, "account is the same as the acronym.  Setting account to blank  " + account);
4924            }
4925            account = EMPTY_STRING;
4926        }
4927        return account;
4928    }

4941    {

4945        }
4946        else

4949        }

4951        if (isICMOrder())
4952        {

4955        else if (clearsLikeQuote())
4956        {

4959            {

4961                //boolean updated = overrideTradeReport(getOptionalData(), reportEntry);

4969                }
4970            }
4971        }

4975        setBrokerAcronymForManulQuote(reportEntry);
4976        
4977        // set sell side indicator for trade report entry
4978        setSellSideIndicator(reportEntry);

4981    private void setBrokerAcronymForManulQuote(TradeReportEntry reportEntry) 
4982    {
4983        if (isManualQuote()) 
4984        {
4985            // get XXP from OrderHomeImpl
4986            String manualQuoteContraOrderBroker = getMyHome().getManualQuoteContraOrderBroker();
4987            ExchangeAcronymStruct manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym 
4988                = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(getUserAcronym().exchange, manualQuoteContraOrderBroker);
4989            
4990            // get XXH from OrderHomeImpl
4991            String anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker = getMyHome().getAnonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker(); 
4992            
4993            //set broker acronym to XXP for manual quote 
4994            //if the contra tradable is an order and its broker acronym is XXH 
4995            if (this.isBuySide() && (reportEntry.getSellOrderId() != 0) 
4996                    && (reportEntry.getSeller() != null) 
4997                    && (reportEntry.getSeller().acronym.equals(anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker)) )
4998                    reportEntry.setSeller(manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym);
4999            else if (this.isSellSide() && (reportEntry.getBuyOrderId() != 0) 
5000                    && (reportEntry.getBuyer() != null) 
5001                    && (reportEntry.getBuyer().acronym.equals(anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker)) )
5002                reportEntry.setBuyer(manualQuoteClearningBorkerAcronym);   
5003        }
5004    }

5009    private void overrideFillReportWithProfile(FilledReportStruct filledReport)

5072    private void overrideTradeReport(String account, String subAccount,

5074                                     TradeReportEntry reportEntry)
5075    {

5081        {

5154    /**
5155     * do NBBO min size guarantee trade report
5156     */
5157    private void doMinSizeGuaranteeTradeReport(TradeReportEntry reportEntry, short tradeContext)
5158    {
5159        String EMPTY_STRING = "";
5160        reportEntry.setSessionName(getActiveSession());
5161        if (isBuySide() || isAsDefinedSide())
5162        {
5163            reportEntry.setBuyAccount(getAccount());
5164            reportEntry.setBuyCorrespondentId(getCorrespondentFirm());
5165            reportEntry.setBuyerUserKey(getUserKey());
5166            reportEntry.setBuyer(getClearingAcronym(tradeContext));
5167            reportEntry.setBuyerCmta(getCmtaFirm());
5168            reportEntry.setBuyerOptionalData(getOptionalData());
5169            reportEntry.setBuyerAuctionTrade(isAuctionTrade());
5170            reportEntry.setBuyerOriginType(getOrderOriginType());
5171            reportEntry.setBuyerPositionEffect(getPositionEffect());
5172            reportEntry.setBuyerSubAccount(getSubAccount());
5173            reportEntry.setBuyFirm(getFirm());
5174            reportEntry.setBuyFirmBranch(EMPTY_STRING);
5175            reportEntry.setBuyFirmBranchSequenceNumber(0);
5176            reportEntry.setBuyOrderId(getUniqueId());
5177            reportEntry.setBuyQuoteId(0);
5178            reportEntry.setBuyOriginator(getOriginatorAcronym(false));
5179            reportEntry.setBuyReinstatable(isReinstatable());
5180            reportEntry.setBuyOrderDate(getOrderDate());
5181            reportEntry.setBuyOrsid(getOrsId());
5182            return;
5183        }
5184        else
5185        {
5186            reportEntry.setSellAccount(getAccount());
5187            reportEntry.setSellCorrespondentId(getCorrespondentFirm());
5188            reportEntry.setSellerUserKey(getUserKey());
5189            reportEntry.setSeller(getClearingAcronym(tradeContext));
5190            reportEntry.setSellerCmta(getCmtaFirm());
5191            reportEntry.setSellerOptionalData(getOptionalData());
5192            reportEntry.setSellerAuctionTrade(isAuctionTrade());
5193            reportEntry.setSellerOriginType(getOrderOriginType());
5194            reportEntry.setSellerPositionEffect(getPositionEffect());
5195            reportEntry.setSellerSubAccount(getSubAccount());
5196            reportEntry.setSellFirm(getFirm());
5197            reportEntry.setSellFirmBranch(EMPTY_STRING);
5198            reportEntry.setSellFirmBranchSequenceNumber(0);
5199            reportEntry.setSellOrderId(getUniqueId());
5200            reportEntry.setSellQuoteId(0);
5201            reportEntry.setSellOriginator(getOriginatorAcronym(false));
5202            reportEntry.setSellReinstatable(isReinstatable());
5203            reportEntry.setSellOrderDate(getOrderDate());            
5204            reportEntry.setSellOrsid(getOrsId());
5205        }
5206    }

5208     /**

5212     */

5220            // such as leg of spread order and simple order. 
5221            sellSideIndicator = getSideValue();
5222        }
5223        reportEntry.setSellSideIndicator(sellSideIndicator);
5224    }

5343 
5344    // NOTE For linkge phase II, this method must be re-visited.
5345    public FilledReportStruct linkageFill(int productKey, long tradeId, int totalQuantity, Price tradePrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, String reportExtensions) throws DataValidationException
5346    {
5347        FilledReportStruct report = null;
5348        int remainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
5349        String exchangeExecIdString = getExchangeExecIdString(reportExtensions);
5350        if (totalQuantity > remainingQuantity)
5351        {
5352            Log.alarm(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got a fill request for order=(" + getOrderIdString() +
5353                ") with exchange/execId=(" + exchangeExecIdString +
5354                totalQuantity + " contracts; it only has " + remainingQuantity + " available.");
5355            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Traded quantity in fill report exchange/execId=(" + exchangeExecIdString +
5356                ") is greater than remaining quantity of the order", 0);
5357        }
5358 
5359        //zero delta qty, no need to check book status
5360        setTradedQuantity(getTradedQuantity() + totalQuantity);
5361        setShipQuantity(getShipQuantity() - totalQuantity);
5362 
5363        if (getInitialTradePrice() == null)
5364        {
5365            setInitialTradePrice(tradePrice);
5366        }
5367        
5368        char billingType = BillingStrategy.parseLinkageTradeBillingType(this);
5369        report = buildFilledReportStruct(productKey, tradeId, totalQuantity, tradePrice, contraParties, billingType);
5370        try
5371        {
5372            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(report.extensions == null ? "" : report.extensions);
5373            extensionsHelper.appendExtensions(reportExtensions);
5374            report.extensions = extensionsHelper.toString();
5375        }
5376        catch (ParseException e)
5377        {
5378            Log.exception(e);
5379        }
5380 
5381        //For rejecting the fill for an outgoing Satisfaction order we need to store exec id and reciept time
5382        //We are using UserAssignedId for that in order history.
5383        if (isLinkageOrder() && !isIncomingLinkageOrder() && getOrderOriginType() == OrderOrigins.SATISFACTION)
5384        {
5385            try
5386            {
5387                ExtensionsHelper helper = getExtensionsHelper(reportExtensions, "for report");
5388                DateWrapper date = DateWrapper.parse(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME, helper.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXECUTION_RECEIPT_TIME));
5389                DateWrapper expireTime = new DateWrapper(date.getTimeInMillis() + FILL_REJECT_TIME);
5390                addValueToExtensionsHelper(helper, ExtensionFields.EXPIRATION_TIME, expireTime.format(DateWrapper.FIX_LINKAGE_DATE_FORMAT_NAME));
5391                report.extensions = helper.toString();
5392            }
5393            catch (Exception e)
5394            {
5395                Log.exception(this, "Could not set the expiration time for the fill reject for order:" + toString(), e);
5396                //continue as this is not critical.
5397            }
5398        }
5399 
5400        if (getRemainingQuantity() == 0)
5401        {
5402            setState(OrderStates.FILL);
5403        }
5404 
5405        if (Log.isDebugOn())
5406        {
5407            Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderIdString() + " got filled with report with exchange/execId (" + exchangeExecIdString + ") for " + totalQuantity + " contracts");
5408        }
5409 
5410        return report;
5411    }
5412 
5413    /**
5414     * This is used to cancel the order when Satisfaction order disposition is given by NBBO Agent. Cancel reason will not be provided here.
5415     *
5416     * @param disposition
5417     */
5418    public int cancelWithDisposition(short disposition)
5419    {
5420        return orderCancel.cancelWithDisposition(this, disposition);
5421    }

5423    public ExtensionsHelper getExtensionsHelper(String someExtensions, String errLogReason)
5424    {
5425        ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper = null;
5426 
5427        try
5428        {
5429            extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(someExtensions);
5430        }
5431        catch (Exception e)
5432        {
5433            Log.exception(this, "Unable to parse incoming "+errLogReason+" string: " + someExtensions +
5434                    " for order (" + getOrderIdString() + ") - creating default extensions helper", e);
5435        }
5436        finally
5437        {
5438            if (extensionsHelper == null)
5439            {
5440                extensionsHelper = new ExtensionsHelper();
5441            }
5442        }
5443 
5444        return extensionsHelper;
5445    }

5447    private void addValueToExtensionsHelper(ExtensionsHelper helper, String key, String value)
5448    {
5449        try
5450        {
5451            helper.setValue(key, value);
5452        }
5453        catch (java.text.ParseException e)
5454        {
5455            Log.exception("Order: Parse exception while trying to set value in extensions helper.  Value not set.", e);
5456        }
5457    }

5483    private String getExchangeExecIdString(String reportExtensions)
5484    {
5485        String execId = EMPTY_STRING;
5486        String exchangeString;
5487 
5488        // Create an extensions helper for the fill report.
5489        ExtensionsHelper fillExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(reportExtensions, "for report");
5490 
5491        switch (getSource())
5492        {
5493            case Sources.LINKAGE:
5494            case Sources.ITS:
5495            case InternalOrderSources.STOCKFIXLINKAGE:
5496                // Get the exec ID
5497                execId = fillExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.CBOE_EXEC_ID);
5498 
5499                // Set the exchange string (for logging the exec id)
5500                exchangeString = ExchangeStrings.CBOE;
5501 
5502                break;
5503 
5504            default: // must be a CBOE source, exec ID is from elsewhere
5505 
5506                // Get the away exchange exec Id.
5507                execId = fillExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.AWAY_EXCHANGE_EXEC_ID);
5508 
5509                // Get the away exchange; set it (for logging the exec id)
5510                ExtensionsHelper orderExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(getExtensions(), "for order");
5511                exchangeString = orderExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXCHANGE_DESTINATION);
5512        }
5513 
5514        return exchangeString + "/" + execId.toString();
5515    }
5516 
5517    public String getExecutingExchange()
5518    {
5519        String executingExchange = null;
5520        switch (getSource())
5521        {
5522            case Sources.LINKAGE:
5523            case Sources.ITS:
5524            case InternalOrderSources.STOCKFIXLINKAGE:
5525                executingExchange = ExchangeStrings.CBOE;
5526                break;
5527            default:
5528                ExtensionsHelper orderExtensions = getExtensionsHelper(getExtensions(), "for order");
5529                executingExchange = orderExtensions.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXCHANGE_DESTINATION);
5530        }
5531        return executingExchange;
5532    }

5552    /**
5553     *  an order needs NBBO protection if
5554     *  1. it is a customer order
5555     *  2. it request for NBBO protection
5556     *  3. NBBO protection is not overriden. NBBO protection can be overriden if
5557     *      > when order is received, the order is not marketable agaist NBBO, in this case
5558     *        the NBBO protection request is automatically overriden
5559     *      > NBBO agent decides to do so
5560     */
5561    public boolean needsNBBOProtection()
5562    {
5563        return isOrderConfiguredToHaveNBBOProtection() && ! isNBBOProtectionOverriden();
5564    }
5565 
5566    private boolean isOrderConfiguredToHaveNBBOProtection()
5567    {
5568            if (isLightOrder())
5569            {
5570                    return isNBBOProtectionRequested();
5571            }
5572        try
5573        {
5574            boolean linkageEnable = getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getTradingPropertyLinkageEnabledFlag();
5575            if (! linkageEnable)
5576            {
5577                return false;
5578            }
5579        }
5580        catch (NotFoundException e)
5581        {
5582            Log.alarm(this, " Could not find the linkage enabled flag for order:" + getOrderIdString());
5583            return false;
5584        }
5585 
5586        short contingencyType = getContingencyType();
5587        
5588        if( contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP ||
5589                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.INTERMARKET_SWEEP_BOOK ||
5590                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.CASH_CROSS ||
5591                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.NEXT_DAY_CROSS ||
5592                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.TWO_DAY_CROSS  ||
5593                contingencyType == ContingencyTypes.TIED_CROSS_SWEEP)
5594        {
5595            return false;
5596        }
5597 
5598        // Internal synthetic order for cross product leg will not need NBBO protection processing
5599        if(getOrderOriginType() == InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER)
5600        {
5601            return false;
5602        }
5603        
5604        String strategy = getMyHome().getIppProcessingStrategy(getActiveSession());
5605 
5606        if (strategy == null)
5607        {
5608            return false;
5609        }
5610 
5611        if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_NONE))
5612        {
5613            return false;
5614        }
5615        else 
5616        {
5617                boolean allow_trd_ship_flag = allowTradeAndShip();
5618                if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_IPP_REQUIRED)  && allow_trd_ship_flag)
5619            {
5620                return true;
5621            }
5622                else if (strategy.equals(OrderHomeImpl.IPP_PROCESSING_IF_CUSTOMER_REQUIRES)  && allow_trd_ship_flag && isNBBOProtectionRequested())
5623            {
5624                return true;
5625            }
5626        }
5627 
5628        return false;
5629    }
5630

5633     * return true if the order has participated in any trade
5634     */
5635    public boolean hasTraded()
5636    {
5637        return getTradedQuantity() > 0;
5638    }

5641     *
5642     */

5649     * @param  aBoolean indicates if NBBO protection should be overriden

5656    /**
5657     * Note: if the new state is ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT, the order is marked with hadNBBOProtection
5658     * true
5659     */
5660    public short changeToState(short aNewState)
5661    {
5662        short oldState = getState();
5663 
5664        if (Log.isDebugOn())
5665        {
5666            Log.debug(this, "changing order state - from: " + oldState + " to: " + aNewState);
5667        }
5668 
5669        if (aNewState == InternalOrderStates.ASSIGNED_TO_AGENT)
5670        {
5671            setHadNBBOProtection(true);
5672        }
5673        else if (aNewState == InternalOrderStates.ROUTED_AWAY) {
5674            setHandlingInstruction(null);
5675        }
5676        setState(aNewState);
5677 
5678        return oldState;
5679    }
5680 
5681    /**
5682     * The order was returned to source (no longer in our book) with the reason.
5683     * Return order with reason on IOSC instead of going thru ORSV2...
5684     */
5685    public void directReturnedWithReason(short returnReason, MarketDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs, boolean incrementTxnNumb)
5686    {
5687            int newSequence; 
5688            if(incrementTxnNumb)

5691            }

5695            }

5697        getMyHome().getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptOrderReturnWithReason.getEventType()).acceptOrderReturnWithReason(
5698                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(), getOrderId(),
5699                                returnReason, getPrimitiveProductKey(), newSequence,
5700                ordHistoryStructs);
5701    }

6004    /**
6005     * adjusts the pending trade quantity
6006     * May mean differently in other child classes; INHERITANCE is BAD
6007     */
6008    public void fillPendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice)

6012    }
6013 
6014    public void fillPendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, char billingType) throws DataValidationException
6015    {
6016        validatePendingTrade(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, false); //false indicates this is just a sub pending trade
6017        int pendingTradeQuantity = getPendingTradeQuantity();
6018        if (pendingTradeQuantity == 0)
6019        {
6020            setPendingTradeQuantity(pendingTradeQuantity + quantity);
6021            setPendingTradePrice(aPrice);
6022            setPendingTradeId(tradeId);
6023        }
6024        else
6025        {
6026            setPendingTradeQuantity(pendingTradeQuantity + quantity);
6027        }
6028    }

6030    /**
6031     * complete a pending trade
6032     */
6033    public FilledReportStruct completePendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, ContraPartyStruct[] contraParties, char billingType)
6034    throws DataValidationException
6035    {
6036        validatePendingTrade(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, true); //true indicates this is a completion call
6037        setPendingTradeQuantity(0);
6038        setPendingTradePrice(null);
6039        setPendingTradeId(0);
6040        FilledReportStruct report = doOrderFill(product, tradeId, quantity, aPrice, contraParties, billingType, true, null);
6041        return report;
6042    }
6043 
6044    /**
6045     * validate pending trade
6046     */
6047    private void validatePendingTrade(int product, long tradeId, int quantity, Price aPrice, boolean inCompletion)
6048    throws DataValidationException
6049    {
6050        String logMSG;
6051        if (getPrimitiveProductKey() != product)
6052        {
6053            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> pending fill product key does not match order productkey" + product + ":" + getPrimitiveProductKey();
6054            Log.alarm(logMSG);
6055            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
6056        }
6057        if (getPendingTradeQuantity() == 0)
6058        {
6059            return; //order is not in a pending trade yet
6060        }
6061        if (tradeId != getPendingTradeId())
6062        {
6063            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Order can only participate in one pending at any given time " + toString();
6064            Log.alarm(logMSG);
6065            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TRADE_TYPE);
6066        }
6067        if (aPrice != getPendingTradePrice())
6068        {
6069            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Sub-pending trades can only occur at the same price in one pending trade " + toString();
6070            Log.alarm(logMSG);
6071            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRICE);
6072        }
6073        if (inCompletion && quantity != getPendingTradeQuantity())
6074        {
6075            logMSG = "OrderImpl >>> Pending trade quantity has to be the same as the sum of quantities of all sub-pending trades";
6076            Log.alarm(logMSG);
6077            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(logMSG, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_QUANTITY);
6078        }
6079 
6080    }
6081 
6082    /**
6083     * To return the OrderBookStruct from the Order.
6084     *
6085     * @return com.cboe.idl.cmiIntermarketMessages.OrderBookStruct
6086     * author Sandip Chatterjee
6087     */
6088    public OrderBookStruct toOrderBookStruct()
6089    {
6090       OrderBookStruct obs = new OrderBookStruct();
6091 
6092       obs.orderId = getOrderId();
6093       obs.originalQuantity = getOriginalQuantity();
6094       obs.remainingQuantity = getRemainingQuantity();
6095 
6096       obs.classKey = getClassKey();
6097       obs.productKey = getProductKey().intValue();
6098 
6099       obs.productType = getProductType();
6100       obs.tradableType = OrderBookItemTypes.BOOK_ITEM_ORDER; // By definition
6101 
6102       obs.side = getSideValue();
6103       obs.price = new PriceStruct();
6104       obs.price = getPrice().toStruct();
6105 
6106       obs.timeInForce = getTimeInForce();
6107        obs.receivedTime = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(getSourceReceivedTime());
6108 
6109       obs.contingency = new OrderContingencyStruct();
6110       obs.contingency.price = new PriceStruct();
6111       obs.contingency.price = getContingencyPrice().toStruct();
6112       obs.contingency.type = getContingencyType();
6113       obs.contingency.volume = getContingencyVolume();
6114 
6115        obs.orderOriginType = getOrderOriginType();
6116        obs.state = getState();
6117 
6118       obs.orderNBBOProtectionType = getNBBOProtectionType();
6119       obs.optionalData = "";
6120 
6121       return obs;
6122    }

6130     private int getLotSize()
6131     {
6132        try
6133        {
6134            return getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getTradingPropertyLotSize();

6136            catch (Exception e)

6139         }

6142     private int getLotSizeForBooking()
6143     {
6144        try
6145        {
6146            TradingProduct tProd = getTradingProduct() ;
6147            TradingClass tClass = tProd.getTradingClass() ;
6148            if (isMarketLotSizeRequired(tClass))
6149        {
6150                return tClass.getTradingPropertyMarketLotSize();
6151            }
6152            else
6153            {
6154                return tClass.getTradingPropertyLotSize();
6155            }    
6156            }
6157            catch (Exception e)
6158            {
6159             
6160            if (SessionNameHelper.isEquitySession(getSessionNameForProduct(getProductKey())))
6161           {
6162               Log.information("OrderImpl - Failed to find lot size for equity session product,defaulting to lotSize = 100. Product key is: " + getProductKey()); 
6163               return 100;    //default property value would be better
6164            }
6165               else
6166               {  
6167               Log.information("OrderImpl - Failed to find lot size for non-equity session product,defaulting to lotSize = 1. Product key is: " + getProductKey());  
6168                   return 1;      //default property value would be better
6169               }    
6170         }
6171      }

6175     {

6179          
6180        
6181         
6182     }

6184     private boolean isMarketLotSizeProduct(TradingClass tc)
6185     {
6186         boolean marketLotSizeProduct = false;
6187          
6188         if (tc.isEquity())
6189         {    
6190             marketLotSizeProduct = true;
6191         }    
6192         if (tc.isIndex())
6193         {    
6194             marketLotSizeProduct = true;
6195         }
6196         return marketLotSizeProduct ;
6197     }

6205    private String getSessionClearingAcronymInProfile(SessionProfileUserDefinitionStruct userStruct)
6206    {
6207        String acr = UNDEFINED;
6208 
6209        if (allowUseClearingAcronymConfigured() && (userStruct != null) && (userStruct.role != UserRoles.MARKET_MAKER))
6210        {
6211            // sessionClearingAcronym is used by Non MarketMaker's order only
6212            // if it is with Market maker role, do nothing
6213            if (Log.isDebugOn())
6214            {
6215                Log.debug(this, "trying to find the default clearing acronym for user: " + userStruct.userId  + ", sessionName: " + getActiveSession() + " for order: " + toString());
6216            }
6217            for (int i = 0; i < userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms.length; i++)
6218            {
6219                if (getActiveSession().equals(userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionName))
6220                {
6221                   acr = userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym;
6222                   if (Log.isDebugOn())
6223                   {
6224                       Log.debug(this, "Needs to overwrite the clearingAcr to: " + userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym +
6225                                       ", of user: " + userStruct.userId + ", sessionName: " + getActiveSession() + " for order: " + toString());
6226                   }
6227                   break;
6228                }
6229                if (SessionNameValues.ALL_SESSION_NAME.equals(userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionName))
6230                {
6231                    acr = userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym;
6232                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
6233                    {
6234                        Log.debug(this, "Needs to overwrite the clearingAcr to: " + userStruct.sessionClearingAcronyms[i].sessionClearingAcronym +
6235                                        ", of user: " + userStruct.userId + ", sessionName: " + SessionNameValues.ALL_SESSION_NAME + " for order: " + toString());
6236                    }
6237                }
6238            }
6239        }
6240        return acr;
6241    }

6256    /**
6257     * Calculates the acronym name for  clearing purpose from profile.clearingAcronym.
6258     * Originator will be used if is for ICM order.  For Other order, if not MM, will try
6259     * to use Broker's clearingAcronym.
6260     *
6261     * @return  The originator acronym if is ICM
6262     *          The Broker's clearingAcronym
6263     *          default if broker has not configured to use the feature.
6264     */
6265    public ExchangeAcronymStruct getClearingAcronym(short tradeContext, boolean isTradeWithManualQuote)
6266    {
6267        ExchangeAcronymStruct tmpUserAcronym = getUserAcronym(); // default to use first
6268 
6269        //If it is an auction trade then ONLY for internalized or matched order return different executing broker
6270        if (tradeContext == TradeContext.AUCTION_TRADE && (isInternalizedOrder() || isFirmMatchOrder()))
6271        {
6272            return getInternalizationAuctionTradeBroker();
6273        }
6274 
6275        String acr = tmpUserAcronym.acronym;
6276        SessionProfileUserDefinitionStruct userStruct = null;
6277        try
6278        {
6279            // if clears like quote use originator's setup (new requirement for I-order 2-25-04), otherwise use user's setup
6280            // WR #6208: manul quote's clearning acronym is its originator's acronym
6281            if (clearsLikeQuote() || isManualQuote())
6282            {
6283                tmpUserAcronym = getOriginatorAcronym(); // this could be the use or the originator is has one
6284                acr =  tmpUserAcronym.acronym;
6285                if (Log.isDebugOn())
6286                {
6287                   Log.debug(this, "Found I-order Originator User(" + tmpUserAcronym.exchange + "-" + tmpUserAcronym.acronym + ") for the operator userId(" + getUserId() + ") for order: " + toString());
6288                }
6289            }
6290            else
6291            {
6292                userStruct = getUserMaintenanceService().getSessionProfileUserByUserId(getUserId());
6293                String newAcr =  getSessionClearingAcronymInProfile(userStruct);
6294                if (UNDEFINED.equals(newAcr) && getMyHome().isAnonymousTradingIfNotClearsLikeQuote())
6295                {
6296                    newAcr = getMyHome().getAnonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker();
6297                }
6298 
6299                if (UNDEFINED.equals(newAcr)  || NOT_APPLICABLE.equals(newAcr))
6300                {
6301                    // Session specific default clearing Acr is not defined for User
6302                    // and anonymousIfNotClearsLikeQuoteBroker is not ON or configured in XML either
6303                    // use the submitter user acr of the order, e.g. don't over-ride it with anything.
6304                    newAcr = acr;
6305                }
6306                else if (isTradeWithManualQuote)
6307                {
6308                    // if order trade with manual quote, 
6309                    newAcr = getMyHome().getManualQuoteContraOrderBroker();   
6310                }
6311                tmpUserAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(getUserAcronym().exchange, newAcr);
6312            }
6313        }
6314        catch (Exception e)
6315        {
6316            Log.exception(this, "Cannot get user in getClearingAcronym() from userMaintenanceService by UserId(" + acr + ")", e);
6317        }
6318 
6319        return tmpUserAcronym;
6320     }

6471            if (theClass.getIndexHybridIndicator() && 
6472                    FirmTradingPropertyHelper.isNewBOBLinkage(activeSession, this.classKey, this.productKey) ) {

6478                        }

6481                return false;
6482            }

6576    /**

6579     * or opposite auction price

6581     * @param book
6582     * @return  return true if
6583     * 1) the Order is IOC Quote-like and remaining qty is cancelled or

6586    public boolean cancelIOCQuoteLikeOrder( boolean needsToCheckMKT, OrderBook book)

6591 
6592    /**
6593     *
6594     * @param self
6595     * @param needsToCheckMKT
6596     * @param book
6597     * @return
6598     * @throws DataValidationException
6599     */
6600    private boolean cancelIOCQuoteLikeOrder(Order self, boolean needsToCheckMKT, OrderBook book) throws DataValidationException
6601    {
6602        int qtyToCancel = getRemainingQuantity();
6603        if ( qtyToCancel <= 0)
6604        {
6605            return true;
6606        }
6607        boolean bookIt = false;
6608        if (getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.IOC)
6609        {
6610                if (book != null && needsToCheckMKT)
6611                {
6612                    bookIt = shouldRemainBooked(book);
6613                }
6614                if (!bookIt)
6615                {
6616                    if (isBooked())
6617                    {
6618                        unbookOrder(self, book, qtyToCancel);
6619                    }
6620                    // have to cancel the IOC order,
6621                    // because the current MKT condition doesn't allow to book it
6622                    cancel(ActivityReasons.USER);
6623                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
6624                    {
6625                        Log.debug("Cancelled and unbooked IOC I order's remaning qty : " + qtyToCancel
6626                                + ", OrderId = " + OrderImpl.orderIdToString(getOrderId()));
6627                    }
6628                    return true;
6629                }
6630        }
6631        return false;
6632    }

7010    private TradingClass getTradingClass(int classKey) throws DataValidationException
7011    {
7012        try
7013        {
7014            if (null == tradingClass)
7015            {
7016                return getTradingClassHome().findByKey(classKey);
7017            }
7018            return tradingClass;
7019        }
7020        catch (NotFoundException e)
7021        {
7022            Log.exception("getClass().getName()", e);
7023            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Trading class could not be found.", 0);
7024        }
7025    }
7026 
7027    /**
7028     * Gets TradingClassHome.
7029     */
7030    private TradingClassHome getTradingClassHome()
7031    {
7032        if (tradingClassHome == null)
7033        {
7034            try
7035            {
7036                tradingClassHome = (TradingClassHome) HomeFactory.getInstance().findHome(
7037                        TradingClassHome.HOME_NAME);
7038            }
7039            catch (Exception e)
7040            {
7041                Log.alarm(this, "Unable to get Trading Class Home.");
7042            }
7043        }
7044        return tradingClassHome;
7045    }
7046 
7047    public int getDisplayQuantity()
7048    {
7049                   setDisplayQuantity();
7050        return displayQuantity;
7051    }
7052 
7053    private void setDisplayQuantity()
7054    {
7055        if( getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE )
7056        {
7057            //Any variable prefixed with "prev" means it holds the value
7058            //that existed prior to changing the order's quantity.
7059            //for example, prevDisplayQuantity is the quantity that was 
7060            //displayed before a trade, now we are updating the display
7061            //quantity to reflect the trade.
7062            final int newRemainingQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
7063            final int displayContingency = getContingencyVolume();
7064            int lotSize = getLotSize();
7065            int delta = newRemainingQuantity - prevRemainingQuantity;
7066            if (isDeltaOddAndOrderFlashing(delta, newRemainingQuantity, lotSize))
7067            {
7068                return;
7069            }
7070            if (displayQuantity>0 && isBooked())
7071            {
7072                if ((newRemainingQuantity==prevRemainingQuantity) && (displayQuantity <= newRemainingQuantity))
7073                {
7074                    return;
7075                }
7076 
7077                displayQuantity += delta;                
7078                         
7079                int replenishThreshhold = getReserveOrderRefreshSize()* lotSize;
7080                
7081                if ((displayQuantity <= displayContingency) && (displayQuantity > replenishThreshhold) && (displayQuantity <= newRemainingQuantity))
7082                {
7083                        adjustOddLotDisplay( lotSize );
7084                    return;
7085                }
7086            }
7087            
7088            displayQuantity = Math.min( newRemainingQuantity, displayContingency);
7089            
7090            adjustOddLotDisplay( lotSize );
7091            
7092            int newReservedQuantity = newRemainingQuantity - displayQuantity;
7093            if( newRemainingQuantity>0 && newReservedQuantity < prevReservedQuantity )  //reserved quauntity is now displayed
7094            {
7095                hasReserveQuantityDisplayed = true;
7096            }               
7097        }
7098        else
7099        {
7100            displayQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
7101            if (treatedLikeQuote())
7102                displayQuantity = LotCalculator.roundLotPortion(displayQuantity, getLotSize());
7103                
7104        }
7105    }
7106    
7107    private final boolean isDeltaOddAndOrderFlashing(int delta, int newRemQty, int lotSize)
7108    {
7109        //delta is an oddPortion
7110        // It is flashing
7111        // There is still a remaining round portion
7112        if((isIPPExposing() || getState() == InternalOrderStates.AUCTION_EXPOSING)  
7113           && LotCalculator.isOddLot(Math.abs(delta), lotSize)
7114           && newRemQty >= lotSize)
7115        {
7116            //If tradable is a reserve odd lot flash termination
7117            //do nothing
7118            return true;
7119        }
7120        return false;
7121    }
7122    
7123    private final void adjustOddLotDisplay( int lotSize )
7124    {
7125       // If displayQuantity > lotSize and has odd portion remove that oddPortion
7126       if (displayQuantity > lotSize)
7127       {
7128           //OddPortion is only displayed if there is no remaining round quantity    
7129           int roundLot = lotSize == 1 ? displayQuantity : LotCalculator.roundLotPortion(displayQuantity, lotSize);
7130           int oddLot = displayQuantity - roundLot;
7131           if (oddLot > 0)
7132           {
7133              displayQuantity -= oddLot;
7134           }
7135       }
7136    }
7137    
7138    public int getPrevReservedQuantity()
7139    {
7140        return prevReservedQuantity;
7141    }
7142    
7143    public int getPrevDisplayedQuantity()
7144    {
7145            return prevDisplayedQuantity;
7146    }
7147    
7148    /**
7149     * WARMING:
7150     * This method is implemented in a way that there could be one and only one caller,
7151     *      which currently is the OrderBookPriceItem,
7152     *          as it totally rely on the accurate sequence of pre-cur-pre-cur-...
7153     *             to guarantee correct book depth summary
7154     *      This method is called every time AFTER the prev* are used,
7155     *          and the cur* become the prev* for later
7156     */
7157    public void savePreviousReserve()
7158    {       
7159            if(getContingencyType() == ContingencyTypes.RESERVE)
7160        {
7161                    //Any variable prefixed with "prev" means it holds the value
7162                    //that existed prior to changing the order's quantity.
7163                    //for example, prevDisplayQuantity is the quantity that was 
7164                    //displayed before a trade, now we are updating the display
7165                    //quantity to reflect the trade.
7166                    prevRemainingQuantity = getQuantityAllowed();
7167                    prevDisplayedQuantity = displayQuantity;
7168                    prevReservedQuantity = prevRemainingQuantity - prevDisplayedQuantity;
7169        }
7170    }
7171 
7172    private boolean isCrossProductLegOrder()
7173    {
7174        return getOrderOriginType() == InternalOrderOriginTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_SYNTHETIC_ORDER;
7175    }
7176    
7177    protected void initializeOrderFillList()

7180    }
7181    /**
7182     * this is called from the OrderHome to persist the order history enteries. This
7183     * method will return true is it added the history entry to this list else
7184     * this will return false and will not add the entry to the list.
7185     */
7186    public boolean addFillReportToList(final FilledReportStruct fillReport)
7187    {
7188        if (Log.isDebugOn())
7189        {
7190            Log.debug("OrderImpl::addFillReportToList >> invoqued for orderId=" + getOrderIdString() + " with productKey = " + fillReport.productKey + ", tradedQuantity = " + fillReport.tradedQuantity + ", leavesQuantity = " + fillReport.leavesQuantity + "  for ASYNC_TRADE or SYNC_TRADE");
7191        }           
7192        if(orderFillList != null)
7193        {
7194            if(isAsyncCreateTradePending())
7195            {
7196                orderFillList.add(fillReport);
7197                if (Log.isDebugOn())
7198                {
7199                    Log.debug(this, "OrderImpl::addFillReportToList order " + getOrderId() + " isAsyncCreateTradePending. FillReport added immediatelly (NOT in commitEvent()) to the list");
7200                }
7201            }
7202            else 
7203            {
7204            Transaction.registerListener(new TransactionListener() {
7205                public void commitEvent()
7206                {
7207            orderFillList.add(fillReport);
7208                }
7209                public void rollbackEvent()
7210                {
7211                }});
7212            }
7213            return true;
7214        }
7215        return false;
7216    }
7217    public FilledReportStruct[] getFilledReports()
7218    {
7219        return orderFillList.toArray(new FilledReportStruct[orderFillList.size()]);
7220    }

7229    public void fill(FilledReportStruct[] filledReports, int startIndex)
7230    throws DataValidationException{
7231        LegOrderDetail legDetail = null;
7232        int preProductKey = -1;
7233        
7234        if(startIndex >= filledReports.length)
7235        {
7236            setTransactionSequenceNumber(filledReports[filledReports.length -1].transactionSequenceNumber);
7237        }
7238        
7239        for (int i=startIndex;i<filledReports.length;i++)
7240        {
7241            FilledReportStruct fill=filledReports[i];
7242            try
7243            {
7244                //for potential use of multiple leg fills
7245                if (fill.productKey != preProductKey)
7246                {
7247                   legDetail = findOrderDetailForLeg(fill.productKey);
7248                   preProductKey = fill.productKey;
7249                }
7250                fill.transactionSequenceNumber = incrementSequenceNumber();
7251                fill.fillReportType = ReportTypes.STRATEGY_LEG_REPORT;
7252                legDetail.setFill(fill);
7253            }
7254            catch (Exception e)
7255            {
7256                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
7257                        "not found the leg with product key = " + productKey + " of strategy "
7258                                + getPrimitiveProductKey() + ": " + e.getMessage(), 0);
7259            }
7260        }
7261    }

7273    public void publishAuctionEvent(AuctionHistoryStruct p_auctionInfo)
7274    {
7275        OrderHomeImpl orderHome = getMyHome(); 
7276        com.cboe.idl.order.MarketDetailStruct[] ordHistoryStructs = buildMarketDetailStructs();
7277        
7278        // for new HAL, we need to reflect the last trade into the NBBO. Not changing IDL for timing issue
7279        // so override NBBOStruct based on book
7280        if (p_auctionInfo.auctionType == InternalAuctionTypes.AUCTION_NEW_HAL  && 
7281                        p_auctionInfo.auctionEventType == ActivityTypes.AUCTION_START) {
7282                
7283            OrderBook orderBook;
7284            try {
7285                    orderBook = getMyHome().getOrderBook(productKey);
7286            } catch(DataValidationException dve) {
7287                    Log.alarm("Failed to overrideNBBOForHAL. Can't get OrderBook for product: " + productKey);
7288                    return;
7289            }
7290            
7291            BestBookStruct bestBookStruct = orderBook.getBestBook().toNonContingentStruct();
7292            Price bboAskPrice = PriceFactory.create(bestBookStruct.askPrice);
7293            Price bboBidPrice = PriceFactory.create(bestBookStruct.bidPrice);
7294                
7295                Price botrAskPrice = PriceFactory.create(ordHistoryStructs[0].botrAskPrice);
7296                Price botrBidPrice = PriceFactory.create(ordHistoryStructs[0].botrAskPrice);
7297                
7298            String CBOEExchangeName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getSession(bestBookStruct.sessionName).exchangeAcronym;
7299                
7300            // if CBOE is no longer NBBO, take BOTR for NBBO
7301                if (ordHistoryStructs[0].nbboBidExchanges.equals(CBOEExchangeName) &&
7302                            new BuySide().isFirstBetter(botrBidPrice, bboBidPrice)) {
7303                    // populate BOTR to NBBO
7304                        ordHistoryStructs[0].nbboBidPrice = ordHistoryStructs[0].botrBidPrice;
7305                        /* quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidPrice = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidPrice;
7306                        quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidExchangeVolume = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidExchangeVolume; */
7307                }
7308                
7309                if (ordHistoryStructs[0].nbboAskExchanges.equals(CBOEExchangeName) &&
7310                            new SellSide().isFirstBetter(botrAskPrice, bboAskPrice)) {
7311                    // populate BOTR to NBBO
7312                        ordHistoryStructs[0].nbboAskPrice = ordHistoryStructs[0].botrAskPrice;
7313                        /* quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidPrice = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidPrice;
7314                        quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct.bidExchangeVolume = quoteQueryV2Struct.quoteQueryStruct.botrStruct.bidExchangeVolume; */
7315    }
7316    
7317                
7318                // overrideNBBOForHAL(ordHistoryStructs[0].quoteQueryForPackageAndLegs.quoteQueryV2Struct, p_auctionInfo.productKey);
7319        }
7320        orderHome.getInternalOrderStatusPublisher(this, InternalOrderStatusEventsEnum.acceptAuctionEvent.getEventType() ).acceptAuctionEvent(
7321                getRoutingStruct(), getOrderRoutingParameterStruct(), getOrderId(),
7322                p_auctionInfo, getTransactionSequenceNumber(),
7323                ordHistoryStructs);
7324      
7325        if (Log.isDebugOn())
7326        {
7327            Log.debug(this, "Order " + getOrderId() + " got auction for " + p_auctionInfo.quantityTradedInAuction + " contracts");
7328        }        
7329    }

7361    public MarketDetailStruct[] buildMarketDetailStructs()
7362    {

7400    public boolean isDeltaNeutral() throws NotFoundException, SystemException
7401    {
7402        LegOrderDetail[] legs = getLegOrderDetails();
7403        boolean stockFlag = false;
7404        int legPriceCount = 0;
7405        // Atleast one leg should be an Equity
7406        for(int i =0; i< legs.length; i++)
7407        {
7408            ProductData legProdData = getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(legs[i].getProductKey());
7409            if(legProdData.getProductType() == ProductTypes.EQUITY || legProdData.getProductType() == ProductTypes.INDEX) 
7410            {
7411                stockFlag = true;
7412            }                       
7413            legPriceCount = legs[i].getMustUsePrice().isValuedPrice()?(legPriceCount+1):legPriceCount;
7414                         
7415        }
7416        
7417        boolean noOrderPrice = getPrice().isNoPrice()? true: false;
7418        
7419        return stockFlag && noOrderPrice && (legPriceCount == legs.length);
7420    }

7442    public String[] getUserIdsFromUserkeys() 
7443    {
7444       String[] dAIMUserIds = new String[this.dAIMedUserList.size()];
7445       for(int i =0; i<dAIMedUserList.size(); i++)
7446       {
7447           try
7448           {
7449               dAIMUserIds[i] = findUserId(dAIMedUserList.get(i).intValue());
7450           }
7451           catch (SystemException e)
7452           {
7453               // don't do anything, no user info available... publish empty string
7454               dAIMUserIds[i] = "";
7455           }
7456            catch (DataValidationException e)
7457            {
7458                // don't do anything, no user info available... publish empty string
7459                dAIMUserIds[i] = "";
7460            }
7461       }
7462       return dAIMUserIds;
7463    }

7554    public boolean needCancelReForUpdate(OrderHandlingStruct update)
7555    {
7556        Price newPrice = PriceFactory.create(update.price);
7557        if (!newPrice.equals(getPrice())) return true;
7558        
7559        if (update.orderOriginType != getOrderOriginType()) return true;
7560        
7561        if (update.side != getSide().toSideValue()) return true;
7562        
7563        if (update.contingency.type != getContingencyType()) return true;
7564 
7565        int newQuantity = update.originalQuantity;
7566        if (newQuantity > getQuantityAllowed()) return true;
7567 
7568        return false;
7569    }

7692    public boolean isProtected()
7693    {
7694        // A / B / C / J / W  are protected
7695        // Except AON orders and OddLots
7696        char origin = getOrderOriginType();
7697        
7698        return (this.getContingencyType() != ContingencyTypes.AON  &&
7699                (origin == OrderOrigins.PRINCIPAL_ACTING_AS_AGENT
7700                || origin == OrderOrigins.BROKER_DEALER
7701                || origin == OrderOrigins.CUSTOMER
7702                || origin == OrderOrigins.FIRM_FBW_ICM
7703                || origin == OrderOrigins.BROKER_DEALER_FBW_NON_CUSTOMER)&&
7704                !this.isOddLot());
7705    }

7712    public void changesCommitted()
7713    {
7714            TradingProduct tradingProduct = null;
7715            
7716            try
7717            {
7718                    tradingProduct = getTradingProduct();
7719            }
7720            catch (Exception e)
7721            {
7722                    
7723            }
7724            
7725            if (tradingProduct !=null && !tradingProduct.isProxy())
7726            {
7727                setBypassReflection(true);
7728                getMyHome().updateToSync(this);
7729                setBypassReflection(false);
7730            }
7731            else
7732            {
7733                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
7734                    {
7735                            Log.debug("Ignoring order sync for PROXY PRODUCT:"+getProductClassKey());
7736                    }
7737            
7738            }
7739    }

8078    private void setOrderSide(char order_side) 
8079    {
8080        if(this.order_side == null)
8081        {
8082            switch(order_side)
8083            {
8084                case Sides.BUY : 
8085                    this.order_side = BUY_SIDE;
8086                    break;
8087                case Sides.SELL :
8088                case Sides.SELL_SHORT :
8089                case Sides.SELL_SHORT_EXEMPT :
8090                    this.order_side = SELL_SIDE;
8091                    break;
8092                case Sides.AS_DEFINED : 
8093                    this.order_side = AS_DEFINED_SIDE;
8094                    break;
8095                case Sides.OPPOSITE :
8096                    this.order_side = OPPOSITE_SIDE;
8097                    break;
8098            }
8099        }
8100    }

8103    {
8104        return order_side;
8105    }

8107    /**********************   Reflection Free Order Related changes   *****************/
8108 
8109    private OrderImplTXChangeLog getCurrentTXLog()
8110    {
8111        TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionLog = Transaction.getCallbackSession().getCurrentTransaction();
8112        TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionParentLog = Transaction.getCallbackSession().getCurrentTransaction().getParentTransaction();
8113        markOrderFieldChanged();
8114        OrderImplTXChangeLog tmpOrderImplTXChangeLog = (OrderImplTXChangeLog) getCurrentTXLog(owRequestedTransactionLog, firstOrderImplTXChangeLog, orderImplTXChangeLog);
8115 
8116        if(tmpOrderImplTXChangeLog == null)
8117        {
8118 
8119            linkMissingOWTransactionLog(owRequestedTransactionLog, owRequestedTransactionParentLog);
8120 
8121            OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
8122            currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(owRequestedTransactionLog);
8123            if(owRequestedTransactionLog != null)
8124            {
8125                currentOrderTXLog.setOwParentTxLog(owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction());
8126            }
8127            currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(orderImplTXChangeLog);
8128            if(orderImplTXChangeLog != null)
8129            {
8130                orderImplTXChangeLog.setChildTXChangeLog(currentOrderTXLog);
8131            }
8132 
8133            orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
8134        }
8135 
8136        if(firstOrderImplTXChangeLog == null)
8137        {
8138            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = orderImplTXChangeLog;
8139        }
8140 
8141        //Log.information("ORDERID: " + this.getOrderIdString() + "OrdeRImpl.getCurrentTXLog >>> FirstTX Log: " + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog + ":" + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog() + ":" + firstOrderImplTXChangeLog.getOwParentTxLog());
8142        //Log.information("ORDERID: " + this.getOrderIdString() + "OrdeRImpl.getCurrentTXLog >>> Current OrderTX Log Log: " + orderImplTXChangeLog + ":" + orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog() + ":" + orderImplTXChangeLog.getOwParentTxLog());
8143        return orderImplTXChangeLog;
8144    }
8145 
8146    private void linkMissingOWTransactionLog(TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionLog,
8147            TransactionLog owRequestedTransactionParentLog)
8148    {
8149        if(orderImplTXChangeLog == null && owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction() != null)
8150        {
8151            TransactionLog tempOWTXLog = owRequestedTransactionLog.getParentTransaction();
8152            while(tempOWTXLog != null)
8153            {
8154                if(tempOWTXLog.getParentTransaction() == null)
8155                {
8156                    break;
8157                }
8158                tempOWTXLog = tempOWTXLog.getParentTransaction();
8159            } //end while loop
8160            
8161            TransactionLog currentCachedOWTXLog = tempOWTXLog;
8162 
8163            //Create OrderImplTXLog for Root Transaction
8164            OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
8165            currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(tempOWTXLog);
8166            currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(null);
8167            orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
8168            
8169            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = orderImplTXChangeLog;       //set the First TX log.     
8170        }
8171        
8172        if(orderImplTXChangeLog != null)
8173        {
8174            TransactionLog currentCachedOWTXLog = orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog();
8175            while(currentCachedOWTXLog != null && currentCachedOWTXLog != owRequestedTransactionParentLog)
8176            {
8177                if(currentCachedOWTXLog.getSubTransaction() == owRequestedTransactionLog)
8178                {
8179                    break;
8180                }
8181                OrderImplTXChangeLog currentOrderTXLog = new OrderImplTXChangeLog();
8182                currentOrderTXLog.setOWCurrentTxLog(currentCachedOWTXLog.getSubTransaction());
8183                currentOrderTXLog.setParentTXChangeLog(orderImplTXChangeLog);
8184                orderImplTXChangeLog.setChildTXChangeLog(currentOrderTXLog);
8185                orderImplTXChangeLog = currentOrderTXLog;
8186                currentCachedOWTXLog = orderImplTXChangeLog.getOWCurrentTxLog();
8187            }
8188        }
8189    }
8190 
8191 
8192 
8193    public void commitChangesAndClearUndoLog()
8194    {
8195        // This is fix the problem for AutoLink orders shipQuantity is 0 
8196        //due to rollback while we publish AutoLink event on a root commit.
8197        if(getShipQuantity() == 0 && transientShipQuantity != 0)
8198        {
8199            setShipQuantityWithoutPublishing(transientShipQuantity);
8200        }
8201        
8202        transientShipQuantity = 0;
8203        
8204        super.commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
8205        firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = null;
8206        orderImplTXChangeLog = null;
8207        changesCommitted();
8208    }
8209 
8210    private void rollbackOrderFieldChanges()
8211    {
8212        boolean isRootTransactionRollback = super.rollbackFieldChanges(this, firstOrderImplTXChangeLog, orderImplTXChangeLog);
8213 
8214        if(isRootTransactionRollback)
8215        {
8216            super.commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
8217            firstOrderImplTXChangeLog = null;
8218            orderImplTXChangeLog = null;
8219        }
8220    }
8221 
8222 
8223    /**
8224     * This method registers for the Transaction Listener if the object
8225     * is not marked dirty and does not contains any changes. If it is
8226     * already marked dirty then this method do nothing. The pusrpose is
8227     * to register the transaction Listener only once for this object during
8228     * the current transaction. The object is marked clean (not dirty) on
8229     * commit(after saving changes) or rollback (after undoing the changes).
8230     */
8231    public void markOrderFieldChanged()
8232    {
8233        if(!isObjectMarkedDirty())  //Already marked dirty object and register for the Transaction Lisenter
8234        {
8235            setObjectMarkedDirty(true);
8236            Transaction.registerListener(new TransactionListener()
8237             {
8238                public void commitEvent()
8239                {
8240                    commitChangesAndClearUndoLog();
8241                }
8242                public void rollbackEvent()
8243                {
8244                }
8245             }
8246            );
8247 
8248            Transaction.registerRollbackListenerWithPriority( BOSessionManager.getDefaultManager().getSession(), new TransactionListener()
8249            {
8250                public void commitEvent()
8251                {
8252                }
8253 
8254                public void rollbackEvent()
8255                {
8256                    rollbackOrderFieldChanges();
8257                }
8258            }
8259            );
8260        }
8261    }
8262
